# Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline — Primitive- and Archetype-Centered Source-Expression Production PRD

**Version:** 1.2.0-draft  
**Status:** DRAFT FOR HUMAN RATIFICATION  
**Prepared:** 2026-07-22

# Document Purpose and Authority

This PRD amends and deepens V1.1. It preserves the Canonical Interview Source Package and source-first batch model while restoring the missing creative architecture: Matrix of Edging, psychological role inside tension, archetype coalitions, Primitive Families and Bindings, Primitive Coalition Contracts, coalition signatures, Edge Products, Guest Voice DNA Final Scripts, Brand Context Version, Voice DNA, Visual DNA, RSCS, CCV, CBAR, SDA, SFL, Distillation Layers, Negative Space, Source Fidelity, and Edge Integrity / Anti-Centroid.

The Pipeline does not treat primitives or archetypes as metadata appended after generation. They build the recipe. Every derivative reaches composition through an approved role-in-tension contract, Primitive Coalition Contract, archetype coalition, and Final Script. Every approved Final Script also compiles a reusable 2D Animation Scene Package; full rendering is triggered by the active archetype template or downstream composition.

The operator supplies source authorization and intended use. The product records provenance and operator scope but does not introduce externally imposed creative-filtering layers that flatten the approved creative direction.

## Authority order

1. Activative Intelligence and Visual Narrative Constitution V1.1.
2. Current Program Control authority and reconciled product status.
3. Current Builder, Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, Studio, primitive, archetype, Brand Context, Voice DNA, Visual DNA, and doctrine authorities after ratification.
4. Ratified decisions D001–D068.
5. This PRD after explicit human ratification.
6. Current implementation and accepted predecessor evidence according to exact dispositions.
7. External-project research evidence after dependency adoption, security, and architecture review.

## Status caution

Implementation remains blocked until current product status and exact source bytes are reconciled. This PRD grants no implementation, cloud, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority.

# Vision and Product Promise

## Vision

Conscious Activations should operate as one Activative source-expression, primitive-coalition, and archetype production system. A real human interview becomes a trusted, richly indexed expression field. The Matrix of Edging identifies the live pressure. Primitive spaces extract faithful transforms. Coalition signatures organize force. Edge Products make the tension execution-ready. Archetype coalitions give the viewer a psychological role inside that tension. JIT Skill writers and Composers compile one Guest Voice DNA Final Script. Composition happens before editing. Atomic Harnesses then realize category-native embodiments of that approved force: source-led short videos, Carousels, SuperVisuals, reusable 2D animation scenes, and separately authorized visual assets.

> **Content activates when it gives the viewer a psychological role inside a tension.**

The system should automate scripting, composition, editing, animation, evaluation, and repair with the precision of a specialized production team while preserving human truth, Activative purpose, source fidelity, Primitive Coalition integrity, archetype geometry, Voice DNA, Visual DNA, Negative Space, Edge Integrity, product sovereignty, and human creative authority.

## Product promise

> Given an accepted Canonical Interview Source Package or Asset Package Spec, current Atomic Harnesses, operator-approved source scope, Brand and DNA context where applicable, and a campaign order, the Atomic Harness Pipeline compiles a role-in-tension, Matrix of Edging result, Primitive Coalition Contract, Coalition Signature, Edge Product, archetype coalition, and Guest Voice DNA Final Script; produces mandatory reusable 2D animation scene programs plus selected source-led short, Carousel, SuperVisual, and VAE jobs; compiles composition before editing; retrieves only coalition-compatible Skills, Steering Recipes, precedents, tools, and Programmed Models; evaluates source fidelity, primitives, archetype fulfillment, Voice/Visual DNA, Negative Space, Edge Integrity, and category grammar; selectively repairs local defects; records human resolutions as programming material; and emits replayable doctrine-to-artifact evidence without changing source or Harness meaning.

## Core operating flow

Activative Interview Brief-led session or imported interview  
→ Canonical Interview Source Package  
→ Brand Context Version / Voice DNA / Visual DNA where applicable  
→ phrase, shot, keyframe, expression, and source governance  
→ Matrix of Edging broad signal and Edge Product formation  
→ Primitive candidate survival and Primitive Coalition Contract  
→ Coalition Signature and archetype coalition  
→ JIT Skill writers and Composers  
→ operator-approved Final Script  
→ composition-before-editing programs  
→ mandatory reusable 2D Animation Scene Package plus category-selected jobs  
→ FFmpeg / Remotion / HyperFrames / Skia / VAE and eligible workers  
→ deterministic, Primitive, Activative, visual, temporal, and DNA evaluation  
→ selective repair or human resolution  
→ source-grounded artifacts, learning episodes, and doctrine-to-artifact receipts

# Users, Jobs, and Journeys

## Primary users

- Conscious Content Operator and creative authority.
- Interview Expression operator and expression-evidence reviewer.
- Primitive Composer, archetype Composer, and JIT Skill script writer.
- Harness Architect and Builder operator.
- Pipeline, static, video, animation, VAE, retrieval, Programmed Model, and evaluator engineers.
- Program Control release and evidence authority.

## Core jobs

- Admit an Activative or imported interview without fabricating history.
- Find the live tension and define the viewer’s psychological role.
- Build the creative recipe from Primitive Families, Bindings, coalitions, and Edge Products.
- Route source expression through a category-native archetype coalition.
- Rewrite text through Guest Voice DNA and approve one Final Script before composition.
- Compose before editing and conduct visual research and real-life reference grounding before generation.
- Produce source-led shorts, Carousels, SuperVisuals, and reusable 2D animation scenes from one source.
- Preserve Source Fidelity, Negative Space, Visual DNA, and Edge Integrity through every handoff.
- Evaluate primitive coverage, misuse, coalition fatality, archetype fulfillment, and anti-centroid charge.
- Supervise campaigns, request exact corrections, and turn accepted resolutions into scoped programming material.

### UJ-01 — Admit an Activative Interview session

The operator uses an approved Activative Interview Brief and recording to create a source package that distinguishes planned activation from actual human expression.

### UJ-02 — Admit an imported interview

The operator uploads existing talking-head footage and transcript and receives the same production entry point without fabricated Brief history.

### UJ-03 — Inspect source expression and form the Edge Product

Hunters propose tags and Expression Moments; Analysts inspect source context; Matrix of Edging compiles surviving primitive candidates, Coalition Signature, and Edge Product; the operator approves the usable source force.

### UJ-04 — Launch one primitive- and archetype-backed content batch

The operator selects outputs, Harnesses, budget, deadline, and autonomy mode; every job binds a viewer role inside tension, Primitive Coalition Contract, archetype coalition, and Final Script obligation.

### UJ-05 — Produce a talking-head short

The original interview footage remains A-roll while an approved archetype-coalition Final Script selects word-safe source spans, captions, overlays, B-roll, and 2D animation scenes; composition is approved before timeline editing.

### UJ-06 — Produce a Carousel

JIT Skill writers and Composers transform approved source expression into a Guest Voice DNA Final Script. The archetype coalition and Primitive Coalition Contract then become a slide-native sequence that gives the viewer a psychological role inside the tension. Verbatim quotes remain explicit; rewritten copy preserves source truth and guest voice.

### UJ-07 — Produce a SuperVisual

One approved Final Script condenses a premise, proof, contradiction, or Edge Product into a primitive-built, feed-legible single-frame argument with active Negative Space, Edge Integrity, Visual DNA, and exact source lineage.

### UJ-08 — Produce reusable 2D animation scenes

Every approved archetype-coalition Final Script compiles a source-grounded 2D Animation Scene Package. The scenes can serve as video B-roll, explainer inserts, quote or concept visualizations, SuperVisual ingredients, or Carousel-slide elements. The active archetype template and downstream compositions determine which scenes are fully rendered. This obligation does not activate deferred Format 02.

### UJ-09 — Acquire a missing visual ingredient

A source-, primitive-, archetype-, and composition-backed demand crosses Delegation to VAE, which may use registered visual capabilities while preserving the approved recipe and Visual DNA.

### UJ-10 — Evaluate and repair a local failure

Rendered output is mechanically checked and independently evaluated against Activative Intelligence contracts, Primitive Evaluation targets, archetype fulfillment, Voice/Visual DNA, Source Fidelity, Negative Space, Edge Integrity, and category grammar; only the responsible unit reruns.

### UJ-11 — Correct production in natural language or by direct manipulation

The Studio compiles the operator’s request or UI delta into a typed ChangeRequestProgram, preserves the active role/tension and coalition contracts, and records the result as a HumanResolutionEpisode.

### UJ-12 — Run in the appropriate autonomy mode

A mature Harness operates in Autopilot or Review Before Ship, while Checkpointed and Shadow modes enforce declared creative gates and publication boundaries.

### UJ-13 — Retrieve the right Skill, primitive-compatible recipe, tool, and precedent

Deterministic filters and hybrid retrieval compile Minimum Complete Context from the active primitive coalition, archetype, Final Script, Brand/DNA context, current composition, and failure state.

### UJ-14 — Promote a Programmed Model claim

A model team builds operator-scoped data from source, primitive, archetype, Final Script, composition, evaluation, and HumanResolution episodes; proves held-out advantage and anti-centroid preservation; shadows the claim; and obtains bounded human promotion.

### UJ-15 — Contain a regression

The system quarantines the affected claim or runtime, routes to a known-good fallback, and restores only after primitive, archetype, doctrine, and technical regression evidence.

### UJ-16 — Ship and audit the batch

The operator accepts or publishes outputs and exports complete source → role/tension → primitive coalition → archetype coalition → Final Script → composition → render → evaluation evidence.

# Canonical Glossary

| Term | Canonical meaning |
|---|---|
| Canonical Interview Source Package | Immutable root object binding source video/audio, transcript, speakers, timestamps, tags, shots, keyframes, Expression Moments, operator-declared source authority, and provenance. |
| Psychological Role in Tension | The role the viewer is invited to occupy—such as witness, recognizer, challenger, learner, confessor, chooser, or participant—inside a meaningful source-backed tension. |
| Matrix of Edging | Force-selection architecture that finds a broad primary signal before elicitation and forms a sharper Edge Product after primitive candidate survival and coalition formation. |
| Primitive Family | A registry family grouping reusable Meaning or Experience Primitive spaces with shared function, activation, suppression, misuse, synergy, and conflict logic. |
| Primitive Binding | Versioned activation of one primitive for a specific role, source evidence, reason, suppression conditions, misuse risks, and evaluation targets. |
| Primitive Coalition Contract | Hashed creative recipe containing primary, support, suppression, and conflict bindings; coalition intent; signature; source context; coverage floor; and misuse threshold. |
| Coalition Signature | Measurable weighted geometry of surviving primitive candidates, family ratios, synergy, redundancy, and routeability. |
| Edge Product | Emergent tension object produced by the coalition and later experienced by the audience; it is not a primitive label. |
| Primitive Evaluation Receipt | Independent record of primitive coverage, misuse risk, coalition integrity, Edge Product survival, decision, and repair ownership for a script, composition, render, or sequence. |
| Primitive Misuse Risk | Probability or evidence that a primitive is absent, excessive, mistimed, contradictory, decorative, or harmful to the active coalition intent. |
| Archetype Coalition Contract | Versioned primary and supporting archetype geometry, viewer role, tension progression, asset-derivative route, category grammar, and source/primitive relationships for one derivative. |
| Final Script | Operator-approved content substrate compiled from source, Guest Voice DNA, Matrix of Edging, Primitive Coalition, archetype coalition, and Distillation Layers before composition begins. |
| Guest Voice DNA | Versioned linguistic organism describing cadence, syntax, compression, pressure, intimacy, metaphor, anti-draft boundaries, and recognizable source-native expression. |
| Visual DNA | Versioned visual organism describing identity geometry, composition tendencies, material language, typography, color, texture, motion, micro-semiotic anchors, and visual Negative Space. |
| Brand Genesis Session | Operator-led process that establishes the brand’s living context, Voice DNA, Visual DNA, acting/identity references, micro-semiotic anchors, and negative-space boundaries. |
| Brand Context Version | Immutable version of the active brand context consumed by scripts, primitives, archetypes, composition, visual production, and evaluation. |
| Distillation Layers | Explicit JIT layers implementing RSCS saturation, collision, compression, evaluation, and recursion from source expression to Final Script and scene programs. |
| RSCS | Recursive Signal Compression Systems: the truth-density engine that distills reality-grounded representations through saturation, collision, compression, evaluation, and recursion. |
| CCV | Combinatorial Controlled Variation: the meaning-expansion engine that recombines compressed truth through explicit archetype, emotion, voice, intensity, maturity, representation, and category axes. |
| CBAR | Constraint-Based Adversarial Reasoning: the hardening engine that resolves tensions between primitive psychology, source truth, category behavior, and implementation physics and proves downstream compatibility. |
| SDA | Semantic Discernment Architecture: shared ontology and grammar for invariants, representation geometry, archetypal geometry, directional integrity, hard negatives, recursive patterns, and feedback loops. |
| SFL | Subliminal Function Layer: registry and crosswalk system for delivery functions, compression rules, surface constraints, archetype/function profiles, and failure corpora. |
| Source Fidelity | Preservation of source truth, context, specificity, uncertainty, voice, and transformation lineage without flattening or invented certainty. |
| Negative Space | Active linguistic and visual structure defining what remains unsaid, unfilled, asymmetric, peripheral, forbidden, or available for viewer participation. |
| Edge Integrity / Anti-Centroid | Preservation of salience, pressure concentration, asymmetry, peripheral force, and meaningful boundary tension against generic mean-reversion. |
| Composition-Before-Editing | Product law requiring approved meaning geometry, primitive coalition, archetype, Final Script, attention path, scene roles, and Negative Space before edit operations. |
| Visual Research Before Generation | Product law requiring category-specific specimen research, contradictions, and visual grammar before provider generation. |
| Real-Life Reference Before Generation | Product law requiring available real-world identity, gesture, material, environment, object, and composition references before synthetic visual production. |
| Steering Recipe | Evidence-backed execution or repair strategy compatible with an already-approved Primitive Coalition Contract, archetype coalition, Final Script, composition state, and embodiment. |
| 2D Animation Scene Package | Mandatory reusable scene program compiled from every approved Final Script for B-roll, explainer, quote, concept, SuperVisual, and Carousel use; full rendering is demand-driven. |

# Doctrine and Product Principles

1. **Activative law:** Content activates when it gives the viewer a psychological role inside a tension.
2. **Interview-First Doctrine:** Production begins by creating or admitting a rich interview source, not by requesting isolated formats.
3. **Expression-First Doctrine:** Actual human expression outranks planned framing, templates, models, and post-production cleverness.
4. **Primitive-First Doctrine:** Primitive Families and Bindings build the creative recipe before Steering Recipes, scripts, layouts, edits, or providers.
5. **Archetype Coalition Doctrine:** Archetypes are psychological geometries and route contracts, not labels or themes.
6. **Final Script Doctrine:** Every composition begins from one approved archetype-coalition Final Script.
7. **Composition-Before-Editing Doctrine:** Meaning geometry, source roles, primitive coalition, archetype sequence, attention path, and Negative Space are approved before edit operations.
8. **Visual Research Before Generation Doctrine:** Visual grammar and contradictions are researched before provider generation.
9. **Real-Life Reference Before Generation Doctrine:** Real identity, gesture, material, environment, object, and composition references ground synthetic production whenever available.
10. **Source Fidelity Doctrine:** Compression and transformation preserve source truth, context, specificity, uncertainty, and voice.
11. **Negative Space Doctrine:** What is absent, peripheral, implied, unsaid, and unfilled is designed and evaluated.
12. **Edge Integrity / Anti-Centroid Doctrine:** Every handoff must preserve salience and meaningful tension against statistical flattening.
13. **Matrix of Edging Doctrine:** Broad signal elicits truth; primitive survival and coalition formation produce the sharper Edge Product.
14. **RSCS Doctrine:** Saturate before compressing; find collision; increase signal density; evaluate reality contact; recurse.
15. **CCV Doctrine:** Expand meaning through explicit controlled axes rather than vague prompt adjectives or seed-only variation.
16. **CBAR Doctrine:** Every Story and runtime behavior is hardened against primitive misuse, implementation physics, and downstream failure.
17. **SDA/SFL Doctrine:** Semantic geometry and delivery function remain explicit, crosswalked, and independently evaluable.
18. **Voice and Visual DNA Doctrine:** Text and visuals preserve the guest and brand organism instead of converging to generic polish.
19. **Mandatory 2D Animation Scene Doctrine:** Every approved Final Script compiles reusable animation scenes; rendering is triggered by archetype and composition demand.
20. **Operator Source Authority Doctrine:** The operator supplies source authorization and intended use; the system records provenance and scope without adding externally imposed creative-filtering layers.
21. **Builder and product sovereignty:** Builder remains canonical; Pipeline executes; VAE produces visuals; Delegation carries cross-product contracts; Studio supervises.
22. **Renderers realize approved programs:** Skia, Remotion, HyperFrames, FFmpeg, animation engines, and providers cannot invent the recipe or accept their own output.
23. **Human Resolution learning:** Every meaningful correction becomes scoped programming material; live doctrine and weights do not self-modify.

# F01 — Product Authority, Brownfield Baseline, and Source Reconciliation

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** The product begins from current constitutional authority, verified product status, and the tested CMF Studio predecessor instead of a greenfield rewrite.

Establish one trustworthy implementation baseline, preserve exact provenance, and prevent predecessor code or stale status from silently becoming current authority. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The owning product is the Atomic Harness Pipeline unless an FR explicitly assigns Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, Studio, Program Control, or an external runtime.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

**Cross-cutting Activative law:** Content activates when it gives the viewer a psychological role inside a tension. Content-bearing work inherits the approved archetype coalition, Primitive Coalition Contract, Final Script, Source Fidelity, Negative Space, Edge Integrity / Anti-Centroid, and Brand/Voice/Visual context when applicable.

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Current Program Control precedence is checked before action.
- Brownfield source use carries exact disposition and provenance.
- Implementation and evidence claims remain separate.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-CUR-001` | `REFERENCE` | CMF_PROGRAM_CONTROL/00_CONSTITUTION/CONSTITUTIONAL_AUTHORITY.md | Constitutional precedence and current product-authority pointer. |
| `SRC-CUR-002` | `REFERENCE` | CMF_PROGRAM_CONTROL/00_CONSTITUTION/current-v1.1/docs/00_ACTIVATIVE_SYSTEM_CONSTITUTION.md | Activation First, Visual Syntax First, product topology and semantic lineage. |
| `SRC-CUR-003` | `REFERENCE` | CMF_PROGRAM_CONTROL/03_PROGRAM_STATUS/MASTER_STATUS.md | Public repository convergence and authorization status observed 2026-07-15. |
| `SRC-CUR-011` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/CURRENT_PROJECT_STATUS.md | Public Builder status snapshot; must be reconciled with newer operator-local receipts before implementation. |
| `SRC-LEG-033` | `RETAIN_EVIDENCE` | docs/audits/CMF_VISUAL_GEOMETRICS_SKIA_SAM3_PRETEXT_AUDIT_2026-06-24.md | Existing execution-spine audit. |
| `SRC-LEG-034` | `RETAIN_EVIDENCE` | docs/prd/modules/PRD_CMF_07_Editing_Composition_Rendering.md | Legacy editing/composition/rendering intent. |

## 5. Workflow integration

Validated upstream state → feature behavior → typed output and receipt → downstream handoff → evaluation, invalidation, and replay.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-001 — Use current authority precedence

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** The Pipeline shall read Program Control authority and the current Builder/VAE/Delegation product boundaries before accepting any executable binding.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Use current authority precedence` within feature F01.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Current Program Control precedence is checked before action.
- Brownfield source use carries exact disposition and provenance.
- Implementation and evidence claims remain separate.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then the Pipeline shall read Program Control authority and the current Builder/VAE/Delegation product boundaries before accepting any executable binding and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** authority/status reconciliation, source disposition, provenance hashes, dependency adoption review, and denial tests, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D001, D002, D003, D004, D027  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-001, SRC-CUR-002, SRC-CUR-003, SRC-CUR-011, SRC-LEG-033, SRC-LEG-034


### FR-002 — Reconcile public and operator-local status

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** Before implementation authorization, the product shall reconcile the public repository status with newer operator-local receipts and publish one current program status.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Reconcile public and operator-local status` within feature F01.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Current Program Control precedence is checked before action.
- Brownfield source use carries exact disposition and provenance.
- Implementation and evidence claims remain separate.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then before implementation authorization, the product shall reconcile the public repository status with newer operator-local receipts and publish one current program status and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** authority/status reconciliation, source disposition, provenance hashes, dependency adoption review, and denial tests, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D001, D002, D003, D004, D027  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-001, SRC-CUR-002, SRC-CUR-003, SRC-CUR-011, SRC-LEG-033, SRC-LEG-034


### FR-003 — Adopt a brownfield-first implementation law

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** Every proposed source module shall carry REUSE, ADAPT, ACTIVATE, REPLACE or ARCHIVE disposition against the predecessor source register.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Adopt a brownfield-first implementation law` within feature F01.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Current Program Control precedence is checked before action.
- Brownfield source use carries exact disposition and provenance.
- Implementation and evidence claims remain separate.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then every proposed source module shall carry REUSE, ADAPT, ACTIVATE, REPLACE or ARCHIVE disposition against the predecessor source register and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** authority/status reconciliation, source disposition, provenance hashes, dependency adoption review, and denial tests, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D001, D002, D003, D004, D027  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-001, SRC-CUR-002, SRC-CUR-003, SRC-CUR-011, SRC-LEG-033, SRC-LEG-034

- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.

### FR-005 — Preserve exact source provenance

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** Forked or adapted files shall preserve archive identity, source path, file hash, dependency provenance and migration decision.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Preserve exact source provenance` within feature F01.

- Implementation and evidence claims remain separate.

- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** authority/status reconciliation, source disposition, provenance hashes, dependency adoption review, and denial tests, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D001, D002, D003, D004, D027

### FR-006 — Require replacement justification

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** A greenfield replacement of a working predecessor component requires an explicit gap, contract mismatch or bounded-cost justification.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Require replacement justification` within feature F01.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Current Program Control precedence is checked before action.
- Brownfield source use carries exact disposition and provenance.
- Implementation and evidence claims remain separate.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then a greenfield replacement of a working predecessor component requires an explicit gap, contract mismatch or bounded-cost justification and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** authority/status reconciliation, source disposition, provenance hashes, dependency adoption review, and denial tests, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D001, D002, D003, D004, D027  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-001, SRC-CUR-002, SRC-CUR-003, SRC-CUR-011, SRC-LEG-033, SRC-LEG-034


## 7. Execution, model, tool, and human responsibilities

Deterministic services own mechanically decidable facts. Programmed Models or bounded Agent Programs may propose or compile behavior only within their evidence-backed claim and node-local tool grants. Independent evaluators inspect judgment dimensions. Humans own new meaning, identity interpretation, unresolved taste, operator source authority, promotion, and publication authority where assigned. The producing model or runtime cannot accept its own output.

When the feature uses a Hunter, Analyst, Composer, or Commander role, the role is an explicit workflow responsibility. It may be implemented by code, a small model, a larger model, or a human. The role name never hides the actual actor or expand its authority.

## 8. Validation and quality gates

Validation must prove both the intended result and the process that produced it. The minimum feature evidence includes authority/status reconciliation, source disposition, provenance hashes, dependency adoption review, and denial tests. Mechanical tests run before expensive model or visual evaluation. Judgment evaluators are calibrated to the exact category and context. Every denial names the cause, owner, and next admissible action. Every accepted mutation emits an immutable receipt and updates only dependent state.

## 9. Risks, mitigations, and stop conditions

| Risk | Concrete consequence | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| Authority drift | A predecessor, external project, UI, model, or renderer is treated as current product authority. | Require exact source disposition, current authority validation, and product-boundary tests. |
| False completion | A synthetic URI, dry-run, unverified command, or model self-report is promoted as a real result. | Require actual files, hashes, independent validation, and artifact-class labels. |
| Over-broad automation | A model or agent gains tools, context, or authority beyond the current node. | Use JIT context, node-local tool grants, sandboxes, and explicit escalation. |
| Hidden mutation | Accepted meaning, source, program, or human preference changes without a versioned record. | Use immutable versions, typed commands, receipts, and selective invalidation. |

**Stop conditions**

- The behavior would create a second semantic or canonical state owner.
- A required source, authority, contract, primitive coalition, archetype, Final Script, runtime, evaluator, or human decision is unavailable or unverified.
- The implementation would treat migration evidence or an external project as current authority.
- The change would imply real output, production readiness, or certification beyond available evidence.

## 10. Planning and implementation handoff

This module is implementation-ready only after its FRs have one primary vertical Story owner, its Stories pass CBAR hardening, its candidate Tech Specs identify exact existing code and target paths, and Program Control issues a bounded Development Capsule. Until then, this module is a product-authority draft.

*This feature module belongs to the Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline PRD V1.1 source-first reconciliation package.*

type: prd_feature_module
product: Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline
prd_id: CA-AHP-PRD-V1.2
feature_id: F02

# F02 — Atomic Harness Intake and Execution Binding

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** The Pipeline consumes the existing AtomicHarnessDefinition and binds it to approved implementations without creating a second Harness truth.

Turn an immutable Builder product into an executable deployment binding while keeping meaning and implementation separate. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The owning product is the Atomic Harness Pipeline unless an FR explicitly assigns Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, Studio, Program Control, or an external runtime.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

**Cross-cutting Activative law:** Content activates when it gives the viewer a psychological role inside a tension. Content-bearing work inherits the approved archetype coalition, Primitive Coalition Contract, Final Script, Source Fidelity, Negative Space, Edge Integrity / Anti-Centroid, and Brand/Voice/Visual context when applicable.

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Builder remains canonical.
- Bindings select implementations but do not mutate Harness semantics.
- Unresolved capability ownership blocks side effects.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-CUR-004` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/src/cmf_builder/domain/atomic_harness_definition.py | Canonical AtomicHarnessDefinition structure and execution-free status. |
| `SRC-CUR-008` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/src/cmf_builder/domain/capability_ownership.py | Current broad Capability Ownership graph and explicit handoff evidence. |
| `SRC-CUR-010` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/src/cmf_builder/workflow/actor_explicit_contracts.py | Execution-free Workflow Node, edge, authority and validation contracts. |
| `SRC-LEG-001` | `ADAPT` | src/ccp_studio/contracts/studio_pipeline_recipe_harness.py | Old recipe/step contracts become a compatibility input to Workflow IR; they cannot define current meaning. |

## 5. Workflow integration

Validated upstream state → feature behavior → typed output and receipt → downstream handoff → evaluation, invalidation, and replay.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-007 — Load exact AtomicHarnessDefinition

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** The Pipeline shall ingest a portable AtomicHarnessDefinition package and verify schema, identity, hash, authority, lineage, category/profile and invalidation state.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Load exact AtomicHarnessDefinition` within feature F02.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Builder remains canonical.
- Bindings select implementations but do not mutate Harness semantics.
- Unresolved capability ownership blocks side effects.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then the Pipeline shall ingest a portable AtomicHarnessDefinition package and verify schema, identity, hash, authority, lineage, category/profile and invalidation state and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** schema/hash validation, graph reconciliation, binding manifest, compatibility tests, supersession and replay, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D006, D007, D008, D032, D033  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-004, SRC-CUR-008, SRC-CUR-010, SRC-LEG-001

# F03 — Workflow Node Execution Kernel and Bounded Role Taxonomy

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** The Pipeline executes explicit Workflow Nodes within governed Phase boundaries and keeps actor, ownership, role, authority, and product boundary distinct.

Provide the smallest auditable unit of execution and represent Hunters, Analysts, Composers, Commanders, humans, deterministic modules, models, and products without hidden ownership. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The owning product is the Atomic Harness Pipeline unless an FR explicitly assigns Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, Studio, Program Control, or an external runtime.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

**Cross-cutting Activative law:** Content activates when it gives the viewer a psychological role inside a tension. Content-bearing work inherits the approved archetype coalition, Primitive Coalition Contract, Final Script, Source Fidelity, Negative Space, Edge Integrity / Anti-Centroid, and Brand/Voice/Visual context when applicable.

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Every node has one declared actor and owner.
- Handoffs are typed and validated.
- Roles never imply authority beyond their assigned node.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-CUR-007` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/src/cmf_builder/domain/category_runtime_rules.py | Category-native runtime plan requirements, evaluation dimensions and repair units. |
| `SRC-CUR-008` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/src/cmf_builder/domain/capability_ownership.py | Current broad Capability Ownership graph and explicit handoff evidence. |
| `SRC-CUR-010` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/src/cmf_builder/workflow/actor_explicit_contracts.py | Execution-free Workflow Node, edge, authority and validation contracts. |

| `SRC-LEG-002` | `ADAPT` | src/ccp_studio/services/pipeline_run_service.py | Reuse run-state behavior after durable-state and receipt reconciliation. |
| `SRC-LEG-003` | `ADAPT` | src/ccp_studio/services/pipeline_step_run_service.py | Map legacy steps to current Workflow Nodes. |

## 5. Workflow integration

Validated upstream state → feature behavior → typed output and receipt → downstream handoff → evaluation, invalidation, and replay.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-013 — Compile phases into Workflow Nodes

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** Each phase shall contain explicit Workflow Nodes that reference the capabilities they realize and the typed handoffs between them.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Compile phases into Workflow Nodes` within feature F03.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Every node has one declared actor and owner.
- Handoffs are typed and validated.
- Roles never imply authority beyond their assigned node.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then each phase shall contain explicit Workflow Nodes that reference the capabilities they realize and the typed handoffs between them and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** graph validation, scheduling tests, handoff conformance, actor/role matrices, and node receipts, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D009, D010, D011, D020, D037  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-007, SRC-CUR-008, SRC-CUR-010, SRC-LEG-001, SRC-LEG-002, SRC-LEG-003


### FR-014 — Declare four independent classifications

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** Every Workflow Node shall declare execution actor, Capability Ownership class, workflow role and product boundary.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Declare four independent classifications` within feature F03.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Every node has one declared actor and owner.
- Handoffs are typed and validated.
- Roles never imply authority beyond their assigned node.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then every Workflow Node shall declare execution actor, Capability Ownership class, workflow role and product boundary and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** graph validation, scheduling tests, handoff conformance, actor/role matrices, and node receipts, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D009, D010, D011, D020, D037  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-007, SRC-CUR-008, SRC-CUR-010, SRC-LEG-001, SRC-LEG-002, SRC-LEG-003

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** Every node attempt shall record inputs, JIT Capsule, implementation, actions, output, validation, status, timing, cost and lineage.

- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** graph validation, scheduling tests, handoff conformance, actor/role matrices, and node receipts, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D009, D010, D011, D020, D037  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-007, SRC-CUR-008, SRC-CUR-010, SRC-LEG-001, SRC-LEG-002, SRC-LEG-003


## 7. Execution, model, tool, and human responsibilities

Deterministic services own mechanically decidable facts. Programmed Models or bounded Agent Programs may propose or compile behavior only within their evidence-backed claim and node-local tool grants. Independent evaluators inspect judgment dimensions. Humans own new meaning, identity interpretation, unresolved taste, operator source authority, promotion, and publication authority where assigned. The producing model or runtime cannot accept its own output.

When the feature uses a Hunter, Analyst, Composer, or Commander role, the role is an explicit workflow responsibility. It may be implemented by code, a small model, a larger model, or a human. The role name never hides the actual actor or expand its authority.

## 8. Validation and quality gates

Validation must prove both the intended result and the process that produced it. The minimum feature evidence includes graph validation, scheduling tests, handoff conformance, actor/role matrices, and node receipts. Mechanical tests run before expensive model or visual evaluation. Judgment evaluators are calibrated to the exact category and context. Every denial names the cause, owner, and next admissible action. Every accepted mutation emits an immutable receipt and updates only dependent state.

## 9. Risks, mitigations, and stop conditions

| Risk | Concrete consequence | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| Authority drift | A predecessor, external project, UI, model, or renderer is treated as current product authority. | Require exact source disposition, current authority validation, and product-boundary tests. |
| False completion | A synthetic URI, dry-run, unverified command, or model self-report is promoted as a real result. | Require actual files, hashes, independent validation, and artifact-class labels. |
| Over-broad automation | A model or agent gains tools, context, or authority beyond the current node. | Use JIT context, node-local tool grants, sandboxes, and explicit escalation. |
| Hidden mutation | Accepted meaning, source, program, or human preference changes without a versioned record. | Use immutable versions, typed commands, receipts, and selective invalidation. |

**Stop conditions**

- The behavior would create a second semantic or canonical state owner.
- A required source, authority, contract, primitive coalition, archetype, Final Script, runtime, evaluator, or human decision is unavailable or unverified.
- The implementation would treat migration evidence or an external project as current authority.
- The change would imply real output, production readiness, or certification beyond available evidence.

## 10. Planning and implementation handoff

This module is implementation-ready only after its FRs have one primary vertical Story owner, its Stories pass CBAR hardening, its candidate Tech Specs identify exact existing code and target paths, and Program Control issues a bounded Development Capsule. Until then, this module is a product-authority draft.

*This feature module belongs to the Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline PRD V1.1 source-first reconciliation package.*

# F04 — Governed Retrieval and JIT Execution Capsule Compilation

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** Every bounded decision receives the smallest constitutionally eligible and task-relevant context.

Combine deterministic eligibility, lexical/dense/graph/visual retrieval, contradiction coverage, and Minimum Complete Context into a receipt-bearing JIT Capsule. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The owning product is the Atomic Harness Pipeline unless an FR explicitly assigns Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, Studio, Program Control, or an external runtime.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

**Cross-cutting Activative law:** Content activates when it gives the viewer a psychological role inside a tension. Content-bearing work inherits the approved archetype coalition, Primitive Coalition Contract, Final Script, Source Fidelity, Negative Space, Edge Integrity / Anti-Centroid, and Brand/Voice/Visual context when applicable.

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Eligibility precedes ranking.
- Similarity never determines authority.
- Required contradictions, exclusions, and unavailable context remain visible.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-CUR-009` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/src/cmf_builder/skills/jit_capsule.py | Existing phase-local JIT Execution Capsule taxonomy and integrity rules. |
| `SRC-CUR-020` | `REFERENCE` | 02_VISUAL_ASSET_EDITOR/prd/05-features/F17-steering-intelligence-cmf-okf-retrieval.md | CMF-OKF, Steering Recipes, hybrid retrieval and Minimum Complete Context. |
| `SRC-EXT-005` | `REFERENCE` | https://huggingface.co/nvidia/Nemotron-3-Embed-1B-BF16 | Text/code dense retrieval candidate after deterministic eligibility filtering. |

## 5. Workflow integration

Validated upstream state → feature behavior → typed output and receipt → downstream handoff → evaluation, invalidation, and replay.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-019 — Declare node context requirements

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** Workflow Nodes shall declare typed context slots, authority, freshness, contradiction and budget requirements.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Declare node context requirements` within feature F04.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Eligibility precedes ranking.
- Similarity never determines authority.
- Required contradictions, exclusions, and unavailable context remain visible.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then workflow Nodes shall declare typed context slots, authority, freshness, contradiction and budget requirements and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** retrieval benchmark, hard-negative tests, context-size reduction, downstream decision lift, and receipts, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D013, D014, D015, D016, D017, D034  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-009, SRC-CUR-020, SRC-EXT-005

# F05 — Durable State, Checkpoints, Replay, Cancellation, and Recovery

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** Long-running multi-product work remains resumable, cancelable, attributable, and recoverable without repeating accepted work.

Persist immutable events and atomic state transitions while separating resume, replay, repair, retry, cancellation, backup, and restore. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The owning product is the Atomic Harness Pipeline unless an FR explicitly assigns Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, Studio, Program Control, or an external runtime.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

**Cross-cutting Activative law:** Content activates when it gives the viewer a psychological role inside a tension. Content-bearing work inherits the approved archetype coalition, Primitive Coalition Contract, Final Script, Source Fidelity, Negative Space, Edge Integrity / Anti-Centroid, and Brand/Voice/Visual context when applicable.

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- State and receipt commit atomically.
- Accepted checkpoints require validation.
- Late results and migrations preserve history.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-CUR-010` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/src/cmf_builder/workflow/actor_explicit_contracts.py | Execution-free Workflow Node, edge, authority and validation contracts. |
| `SRC-CUR-017` | `REFERENCE` | 02_VISUAL_ASSET_EDITOR/prd/05-features/F10-event-sourced-production-runtime.md | Event-sourced VAE production runtime. |
| `SRC-LEG-002` | `ADAPT` | src/ccp_studio/services/pipeline_run_service.py | Reuse run-state behavior after durable-state and receipt reconciliation. |
| `SRC-LEG-003` | `ADAPT` | src/ccp_studio/services/pipeline_step_run_service.py | Map legacy steps to current Workflow Nodes. |

## 5. Workflow integration

Validated upstream state → feature behavior → typed output and receipt → downstream handoff → evaluation, invalidation, and replay.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-025 — Persist immutable execution events

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** The Pipeline shall persist run, node, handoff, command, receipt and incident events in durable storage.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Persist immutable execution events` within feature F05.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- State and receipt commit atomically.
- Accepted checkpoints require validation.
- Late results and migrations preserve history.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then the Pipeline shall persist run, node, handoff, command, receipt and incident events in durable storage and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** transaction tests, duplicate/retry races, cancellation, replay, backup/restore, and migration evidence, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D011, D032, D037, D038  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-010, SRC-CUR-017, SRC-LEG-002, SRC-LEG-003


### FR-026 — Commit state and receipt atomically

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** A lifecycle transition and its receipt-bearing command record shall commit as one atomic operation.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Commit state and receipt atomically` within feature F05.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- State and receipt commit atomically.
- Accepted checkpoints require validation.
- Late results and migrations preserve history.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then a lifecycle transition and its receipt-bearing command record shall commit as one atomic operation and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** transaction tests, duplicate/retry races, cancellation, replay, backup/restore, and migration evidence, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D011, D032, D037, D038  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-010, SRC-CUR-017, SRC-LEG-002, SRC-LEG-003


### FR-027 — Create accepted checkpoints only after validation

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** A node checkpoint becomes reusable only after output validation, evidence emission and downstream eligibility pass.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Create accepted checkpoints only after validation` within feature F05.

- Late results and migrations preserve history.

- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** transaction tests, duplicate/retry races, cancellation, replay, backup/restore, and migration evidence, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D011, D032, D037, D038

### FR-028 — Separate resume from replay

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** Resume continues from the last accepted checkpoint; replay reconstructs exact historical execution from immutable identities.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Separate resume from replay` within feature F05.

- Accepted checkpoints require validation.

### FR-029 — Govern cancellation and race resolution

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** Cancellation shall prevent new work, propagate to active products/runtimes and disposition late results without losing history.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Govern cancellation and race resolution` within feature F05.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

- State and receipt commit atomically.
- Accepted checkpoints require validation.
- Late results and migrations preserve history.

- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** transaction tests, duplicate/retry races, cancellation, replay, backup/restore, and migration evidence, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D011, D032, D037, D038  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-010, SRC-CUR-017, SRC-LEG-002, SRC-LEG-003


### FR-030 — Provide migration, backup and restore

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** State schemas shall support controlled migration, unsupported-version containment, backup, restore and disaster-recovery tests.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Provide migration, backup and restore` within feature F05.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

- State and receipt commit atomically.
- Accepted checkpoints require validation.
- Late results and migrations preserve history.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then state schemas shall support controlled migration, unsupported-version containment, backup, restore and disaster-recovery tests and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** transaction tests, duplicate/retry races, cancellation, replay, backup/restore, and migration evidence, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D011, D032, D037, D038  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-010, SRC-CUR-017, SRC-LEG-002, SRC-LEG-003


## 7. Execution, model, tool, and human responsibilities

Deterministic services own mechanically decidable facts. Programmed Models or bounded Agent Programs may propose or compile behavior only within their evidence-backed claim and node-local tool grants. Independent evaluators inspect judgment dimensions. Humans own new meaning, identity interpretation, unresolved taste, operator source authority, promotion, and publication authority where assigned. The producing model or runtime cannot accept its own output.

When the feature uses a Hunter, Analyst, Composer, or Commander role, the role is an explicit workflow responsibility. It may be implemented by code, a small model, a larger model, or a human. The role name never hides the actual actor or expand its authority.

## 8. Validation and quality gates

Validation must prove both the intended result and the process that produced it. The minimum feature evidence includes transaction tests, duplicate/retry races, cancellation, replay, backup/restore, and migration evidence. Mechanical tests run before expensive model or visual evaluation. Judgment evaluators are calibrated to the exact category and context. Every denial names the cause, owner, and next admissible action. Every accepted mutation emits an immutable receipt and updates only dependent state.

## 9. Risks, mitigations, and stop conditions

| Risk | Concrete consequence | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| Authority drift | A predecessor, external project, UI, model, or renderer is treated as current product authority. | Require exact source disposition, current authority validation, and product-boundary tests. |
| False completion | A synthetic URI, dry-run, unverified command, or model self-report is promoted as a real result. | Require actual files, hashes, independent validation, and artifact-class labels. |
| Over-broad automation | A model or agent gains tools, context, or authority beyond the current node. | Use JIT context, node-local tool grants, sandboxes, and explicit escalation. |
| Hidden mutation | Accepted meaning, source, program, or human preference changes without a versioned record. | Use immutable versions, typed commands, receipts, and selective invalidation. |

**Stop conditions**

- The behavior would create a second semantic or canonical state owner.
- A required source, authority, contract, primitive coalition, archetype, Final Script, runtime, evaluator, or human decision is unavailable or unverified.
- The implementation would treat migration evidence or an external project as current authority.
- The change would imply real output, production readiness, or certification beyond available evidence.

## 10. Planning and implementation handoff

This module is implementation-ready only after its FRs have one primary vertical Story owner, its Stories pass CBAR hardening, its candidate Tech Specs identify exact existing code and target paths, and Program Control issues a bounded Development Capsule. Until then, this module is a product-authority draft.

*This feature module belongs to the Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline PRD V1.1 source-first reconciliation package.*

title: "Skills, Skill Composition Recipes, Steering Recipes, and Transformation Contracts"

# F06 — Skills, Skill Composition Recipes, Steering Recipes, and Transformation Contracts

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** Stable Skills execute doctrine while Primitive Coalitions build the creative recipe, archetype coalitions organize psychological geometry, and Steering Recipes operationalize or repair the approved coalition.

Let Atomic Harnesses activate reusable Skills without confusing procedure with creative force. Primitive Families and Bindings build the recipe; the Primitive Coalition Contract and archetype coalition establish force and psychological role; Steering Recipes supply evidence-backed methods for realizing or repairing that recipe in a specific embodiment. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The owning product is the Atomic Harness Pipeline unless an FR explicitly assigns Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, Studio, Program Control, or an external runtime.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

**Cross-cutting Activative law:** Content activates when it gives the viewer a psychological role inside a tension. Content-bearing work inherits the approved archetype coalition, Primitive Coalition Contract, Final Script, Source Fidelity, Negative Space, Edge Integrity / Anti-Centroid, and Brand/Voice/Visual context when applicable.

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Canonical Skills are not mutated by local adaptations.
- Primitive Coalition Contracts precede and govern Steering Recipes.
- Archetype coalitions and approved Final Scripts precede composition.
- Recipes carry applicability, primitive compatibility, and lifecycle.
- Transformation Contracts protect meaning while declaring creative freedom.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-CUR-009` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/src/cmf_builder/skills/jit_capsule.py | Existing phase-local JIT Execution Capsule taxonomy and integrity rules. |
| `SRC-CUR-020` | `REFERENCE` | 02_VISUAL_ASSET_EDITOR/prd/05-features/F17-steering-intelligence-cmf-okf-retrieval.md | CMF-OKF, Steering Recipes, hybrid retrieval and Minimum Complete Context. |

## 5. Workflow integration

Validated upstream state → feature behavior → typed output and receipt → downstream handoff → evaluation, invalidation, and replay.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-031 — Bind Canonical Skills explicitly

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** A learned or agentic Workflow Node shall reference the exact Canonical Skill governing its stable procedure.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Bind Canonical Skills explicitly` within feature F06.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Canonical Skills are not mutated by local adaptations.
- Primitive Coalition Contracts precede and govern Steering Recipes.
- Archetype coalitions and approved Final Scripts precede composition.
- Recipes carry applicability, primitive compatibility, and lifecycle.
- Transformation Contracts protect meaning while declaring creative freedom.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then a learned or agentic Workflow Node shall reference the exact Canonical Skill governing its stable procedure and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** skill/recipe binding tests, eligibility/exclusion, recipe lifecycle, transformation validation, and retrieval receipts, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D007, D016, D019, D023, D024, D026  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-009, SRC-CUR-020
