# F16 — Independent Evaluation, Visual Syntax Reparse, Diagnosis, and Selective Repair

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** Production output is mechanically verified, independently evaluated, attributed to the responsible layer, and locally repaired.

Separate deterministic facts from judgment, compare intended and observed composition/timing, and preserve already-valid work. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The owning product is the Atomic Harness Pipeline unless an FR explicitly assigns Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, Studio, Program Control, or an external runtime.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

**Cross-cutting Activative law:** Content activates when it gives the viewer a psychological role inside a tension. Content-bearing work inherits the approved archetype coalition, Primitive Coalition Contract, Final Script, Source Fidelity, Negative Space, Edge Integrity / Anti-Centroid, and Brand/Voice/Visual context when applicable.

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Producer cannot approve itself.
- Failure attribution distinguishes retrieval/model/tool/runtime/evaluator.
- Repair changes only permitted units.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-091 — Verify mechanically decidable conditions

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** Contracts, geometry, text fit, timing, source lineage, tool use, export and execution-envelope conditions shall use deterministic verification.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Verify mechanically decidable conditions` within feature F16.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Producer cannot approve itself.
- Failure attribution distinguishes retrieval/model/tool/runtime/evaluator.
- Repair changes only permitted units.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then contracts, geometry, text fit, timing, source lineage, tool use, export and execution-envelope conditions shall use deterministic verification and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** deterministic validators, evaluator calibration, rendered reparse, diagnosis accuracy, selective rerun, and escalation, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D023, D024, D025, D035, D036, D040  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-018, SRC-CUR-019, SRC-LEG-019, SRC-LEG-020, SRC-LEG-021, SRC-LEG-022, SRC-LEG-023


### FR-092 — Evaluate judgment dimensions independently

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** Separate evaluators shall assess source fidelity, psychological-role clarity, Edge Product survival, Activative function, Primitive Coalition coverage and misuse, archetype fulfillment, Voice DNA, Visual DNA, category-native grammar, Negative Space, Edge Integrity, composition, temporal effect, and wrong-reading risk.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Evaluate judgment dimensions independently` within feature F16.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Producer cannot approve itself.
- Failure attribution distinguishes retrieval/model/tool/runtime/evaluator.
- Repair changes only permitted units.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then separate evaluators shall assess semantic fidelity, Activative function, category-native grammar, composition, temporal effect and wrong-reading risk and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** deterministic validators, evaluator calibration, rendered reparse, diagnosis accuracy, selective rerun, and escalation, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

### FR-093 — Reparse rendered Visual Syntax

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** Static and temporal outputs shall be parsed back into observed BBOX, hierarchy, reading-order and timing evidence for comparison with the intended contract.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Reparse rendered Visual Syntax` within feature F16.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Producer cannot approve itself.
- Failure attribution distinguishes retrieval/model/tool/runtime/evaluator.
- Repair changes only permitted units.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then static and temporal outputs shall be parsed back into observed BBOX, hierarchy, reading-order and timing evidence for comparison with the intended contract and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** deterministic validators, evaluator calibration, rendered reparse, diagnosis accuracy, selective rerun, and escalation, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D023, D024, D025, D035, D036, D040  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-018, SRC-CUR-019, SRC-LEG-019, SRC-LEG-020, SRC-LEG-021, SRC-LEG-022, SRC-LEG-023


### FR-094 — Attribute failures to responsible layers

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** Diagnosis shall distinguish knowledge, retrieval, context, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, VAE and evaluator defects.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Attribute failures to responsible layers` within feature F16.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Producer cannot approve itself.
- Failure attribution distinguishes retrieval/model/tool/runtime/evaluator.
- Repair changes only permitted units.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then diagnosis shall distinguish knowledge, retrieval, context, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, VAE and evaluator defects and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** deterministic validators, evaluator calibration, rendered reparse, diagnosis accuracy, selective rerun, and escalation, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D023, D024, D025, D035, D036, D040  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-018, SRC-CUR-019, SRC-LEG-019, SRC-LEG-020, SRC-LEG-021, SRC-LEG-022, SRC-LEG-023


### FR-095 — Repair only declared units

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** A repair shall change only the diagnosed unit and its permitted dependent units while preserving already-valid relationships.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Repair only declared units` within feature F16.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Producer cannot approve itself.
- Failure attribution distinguishes retrieval/model/tool/runtime/evaluator.
- Repair changes only permitted units.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then a repair shall change only the diagnosed unit and its permitted dependent units while preserving already-valid relationships and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** deterministic validators, evaluator calibration, rendered reparse, diagnosis accuracy, selective rerun, and escalation, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D023, D024, D025, D035, D036, D040  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-018, SRC-CUR-019, SRC-LEG-019, SRC-LEG-020, SRC-LEG-021, SRC-LEG-022, SRC-LEG-023


### FR-096 — Escalate human-owned conflicts

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** Unresolved taste, new meaning, identity/operator source authorization and policy exceptions shall route to attributable human authority.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Escalate human-owned conflicts` within feature F16.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Producer cannot approve itself.
- Failure attribution distinguishes retrieval/model/tool/runtime/evaluator.
- Repair changes only permitted units.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then unresolved taste, new meaning, identity/operator source authorization and policy exceptions shall route to attributable human authority and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** deterministic validators, evaluator calibration, rendered reparse, diagnosis accuracy, selective rerun, and escalation, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D023, D024, D025, D035, D036, D040  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-018, SRC-CUR-019, SRC-LEG-019, SRC-LEG-020, SRC-LEG-021, SRC-LEG-022, SRC-LEG-023


## 7. Execution, model, tool, and human responsibilities

Deterministic services own mechanically decidable facts. Programmed Models or bounded Agent Programs may propose or compile behavior only within their evidence-backed claim and node-local tool grants. Independent evaluators inspect judgment dimensions. Humans own new meaning, identity interpretation, unresolved taste, operator source authority, promotion, and publication authority where assigned. The producing model or runtime cannot accept its own output.

When the feature uses a Hunter, Analyst, Composer, or Commander role, the role is an explicit workflow responsibility. It may be implemented by code, a small model, a larger model, or a human. The role name never hides the actual actor or expand its authority.

## 8. Validation and quality gates

Validation must prove both the intended result and the process that produced it. The minimum feature evidence includes deterministic validators, evaluator calibration, rendered reparse, diagnosis accuracy, selective rerun, and escalation. Mechanical tests run before expensive model or visual evaluation. Judgment evaluators are calibrated to the exact category and context. Every denial names the cause, owner, and next admissible action. Every accepted mutation emits an immutable receipt and updates only dependent state.

## 9. Risks, mitigations, and stop conditions

| Risk | Concrete consequence | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| Authority drift | A predecessor, external project, UI, model, or renderer is treated as current product authority. | Require exact source disposition, current authority validation, and product-boundary tests. |
| False completion | A synthetic URI, dry-run, unverified command, or model self-report is promoted as a real result. | Require actual files, hashes, independent validation, and artifact-class labels. |
| Over-broad automation | A model or agent gains tools, context, or authority beyond the current node. | Use JIT context, node-local tool grants, sandboxes, and explicit escalation. |
| Hidden mutation | Accepted meaning, source, program, or human preference changes without a versioned record. | Use immutable versions, typed commands, receipts, and selective invalidation. |

**Stop conditions**

- The behavior would create a second semantic or canonical state owner.
- A required source, authority, contract, primitive coalition, archetype, Final Script, runtime, evaluator, or human decision is unavailable or unverified.
- The implementation would treat migration evidence or an external project as current authority.
- The change would imply real output, production readiness, or certification beyond available evidence.

## 10. Planning and implementation handoff

This module is implementation-ready only after its FRs have one primary vertical Story owner, its Stories pass CBAR hardening, its candidate Tech Specs identify exact existing code and target paths, and Program Control issues a bounded Development Capsule. Until then, this module is a product-authority draft.

*This feature module belongs to the Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline PRD V1.1 source-first reconciliation package.*

prd_id: CA-AHP-PRD-V1.2
feature_id: F17
title: "Evidence, Human Resolution, Steering Intelligence, and Programmed Model Learning Flywheel"

# F17 — Evidence, Human Resolution, Steering Intelligence, and Programmed Model Learning Flywheel

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** Every production and human-resolution episode strengthens explicit knowledge and offline learned capability evidence without live uncontrolled mutation.

Capture exact before/after state, attribute causes, build operator-authorized datasets, promote recipes and models through evidence, and retain rollback. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The owning product is the Atomic Harness Pipeline unless an FR explicitly assigns Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, Studio, Program Control, or an external runtime.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

**Cross-cutting Activative law:** Content activates when it gives the viewer a psychological role inside a tension. Content-bearing work inherits the approved archetype coalition, Primitive Coalition Contract, Final Script, Source Fidelity, Negative Space, Edge Integrity / Anti-Centroid, and Brand/Voice/Visual context when applicable.

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Capture/indexing is automatic; promotion is not.
- Human preference is scoped.
- Source authority and operator source authorization govern learning.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-CUR-020` | `REFERENCE` | 02_VISUAL_ASSET_EDITOR/prd/05-features/F17-steering-intelligence-cmf-okf-retrieval.md | CMF-OKF, Steering Recipes, hybrid retrieval and Minimum Complete Context. |
| `SRC-AM-001` | `AMENDMENT_INPUT` | CONSCIOUS_ACTIVATIONS_STUDIO_ARCHITECTURE_AMENDMENT_V2_1(2).zip | Format 02 deferral, HumanResolutionEpisode, supervisory Studio, autonomy modes, timeline adoption, and Revision Compiler. |
| `SRC-AM-002` | `AMENDMENT_INPUT` | PA_AM_001_SEVEN_DAY_PARALLEL_PRODUCTION_ACTIVATION_V1_1(2).zip | Parallel Pipeline, temporal, static, VAE, Interview Expression, GNM, and retrieval/model-program activation lanes. |
| `SRC-EXT-001` | `REFERENCE` | file:///mnt/data/Agentic Prompt Enhancer for Image Generation and.pdf | Trainable small prompt enhancers; router–rewriter–composer and downstream-output reward. |
| `SRC-EXT-005` | `REFERENCE` | https://huggingface.co/nvidia/Nemotron-3-Embed-1B-BF16 | Text/code dense retrieval candidate after deterministic eligibility filtering. |

## 5. Workflow integration

Validated upstream state → feature behavior → typed output and receipt → downstream handoff → evaluation, invalidation, and replay.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-097 — Persist complete production and human-resolution episodes

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Each accepted, rejected, repaired, escalated, and human-resolved production episode shall link the source package, Harness, run state, JIT Capsule, candidates, exact tool operations, renders, evaluations, decision authority, result, and downstream outcome.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A node, candidate portfolio, operator action, or campaign reaches a decision or terminal state.

**Required output or state transition:** Immutable ProductionEpisode and, where human authority acted, HumanResolutionEpisode records.

**Authority and invariants:**
- UI actions cannot disappear as anonymous state.
- Human scope and rationale remain explicit.
- No episode mutates live models or canonical doctrine.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given an operator moves a cut and accepts the preview, when the action commits, then the episode records before/after program state, exact tool command, affected nodes, evaluation, and acceptance scope.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a manual change with no attributable authority or before-state identity, when persistence is requested, then the change cannot become accepted state.
- **Evidence required:** Episode hash, before/after references, tool/process receipts, human authority, and result lineage.

**Governing decisions:** D017, D024, D025, D026, D047  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-020, SRC-AM-001, SRC-AM-002


### FR-098 — Attribute learning opportunities to the responsible layer

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The system shall diagnose whether an episode indicates a source, knowledge, retrieval, context, Skill, Steering Recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, VAE, evaluator, or human-policy opportunity before it enters any learning queue.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A production or human-resolution episode is closed.

**Required output or state transition:** A typed attribution record, candidate programming-material dispositions, and excluded interpretations.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Visible symptoms are not automatically assigned to the model.
- Attribution can remain uncertain or multi-causal.
- Promotion requires later evidence.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a bad crop caused by a wrong geometry measurement, when diagnosis runs, then the episode is attributed to measurement/runtime rather than used to teach a taste model.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a single operator rejection with no reason, when attribution is ambiguous, then the system stores it as scoped preference evidence but does not promote a universal recipe.
- **Evidence required:** Diagnosis report, responsible-layer confidence, excluded alternatives, and human review where required.

**Governing decisions:** D017, D024, D025, D026, D047  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-020, SRC-AM-001, SRC-EXT-001, SRC-EXT-005


### FR-099 — Compile operator-authorized versioned programming-material corpora

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Supervised demonstrations, preference pairs, hard negatives, repair trajectories, retrieval-obedience cases, and revision-program examples shall be built offline from eligible episodes with exact source authority, operator source authorization, provenance, scope, splits, hashes, and invalidation.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A model or evaluator team requests a dataset build for a bounded capability claim.

**Required output or state transition:** Versioned corpus manifest, training/validation/test partitions, exclusions, source authority/operator source authorization scope, and source episode references.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Real-human source authority govern downstream training.
- Protected test data is isolated.
- No live-production mutation occurs.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given approved video-revision episodes, when a corpus is built, then source authority and identity scope are checked and the test split remains unavailable to the producer.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given an episode whose operator source authorization does not permit model training, when dataset selection runs, then it is excluded while remaining available for allowed operational audit if permitted.
- **Evidence required:** Dataset manifest, operator-declared source authority report, split hashes, deduplication, leakage tests, and build receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D017, D024, D025, D026, D047  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-020, SRC-AM-001


### FR-100 — Capture human preferences and corrections with explicit scope

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Every operator approval, rejection, candidate selection, natural-language revision, direct manipulation, tool override, taste explanation, and publication decision shall produce a HumanResolutionEpisode whose applicability scope is explicit and nonuniversal by default.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A human takes an authorized action in any Studio surface or review queue.

**Required output or state transition:** A HumanResolutionEpisode with request, before/after state, operations, reasons, authority, learning scope, and candidate dispositions.

**Authority and invariants:**
- One decision never silently becomes universal doctrine.
- Direct UI manipulation and text requests produce equivalent evidence quality.
- Human identity is never synthesized on replay.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a Carousel slide reorder, when the operator commits it, then the exact order change and stated reason are recorded with category/profile scope.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given an operator drag event without a resolved project/run/authority identity, when commit is attempted, then the UI must request resolution rather than writing anonymous state.
- **Evidence required:** Episode record, authority scope, exact changes, tool program, evaluation, and acceptance.

**Governing decisions:** D017, D024, D025, D026, D047  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-001, SRC-AM-002


### FR-101 — Promote Steering Recipes only through repeated evidence

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Repeated successful, scoped interventions may advance a Steering Recipe through proposed, experimental, validated, shadow, limited-production, production, deprecated, and retired states with control comparisons, regression cases, human authority, and rollback.

**Trigger and preconditions:** Episode analysis identifies a recurring condition/intervention pattern.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned Steering Recipe proposal or lifecycle transition with applicability, preserved properties, evidence, controls, failures, and rollback.

**Authority and invariants:**
- A raw winning prompt is not a recipe.
- A single success cannot change defaults.
- Contradictory and failed evidence remains linked.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given ten comparable hierarchy repairs and controls showing consistent improvement, when promotion is reviewed, then the recipe may enter shadow with exact scope and rollback.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given one visually appealing result and no control or failure cases, when promotion is requested, then the recipe remains proposed.
- **Evidence required:** Recipe evidence ledger, control comparison, regression suite, human promotion receipt, and rollback package.

**Governing decisions:** D017, D024, D025, D026, D047  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-020, SRC-AM-001


### FR-102 — Prohibit uncontrolled online mutation while enabling automatic evidence capture

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Production may automatically append immutable episodes, retrieval indexes, and programming-material eligibility records, but it shall not rewrite model weights, canonical Skills, Steering Recipes, authority rules, or production defaults without an offline evaluated release and human authorization.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A production episode or human correction completes.

**Required output or state transition:** Automatic evidence/index updates and, separately, an offline promotion candidate if eligible.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Capture is automatic; promotion is not.
- Historical evidence remains immutable.
- Release rollback is always possible.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given an accepted correction, when the episode closes, then retrieval can find it immediately while the production model remains unchanged.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a service attempting to update an adapter checkpoint directly from a live click stream, when policy enforcement runs, then the mutation is blocked and incident evidence is recorded.
- **Evidence required:** Mutation-denial tests, index update receipt, model artifact immutability checks, and promotion workflow.

**Governing decisions:** D017, D024, D025, D026, D047  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-020, SRC-AM-001

# F18 — Execution Fingerprints, Sandbox, Continuous Assurance, and Incident Containment

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** The system proves what executed and contains regressions without blanket recertification.

Record authorized and resolved execution stacks, enforce least-authority sandboxes, monitor signals, and restore known-good implementations. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The owning product is the Atomic Harness Pipeline unless an FR explicitly assigns Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, Studio, Program Control, or an external runtime.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

**Cross-cutting Activative law:** Content activates when it gives the viewer a psychological role inside a tension. Content-bearing work inherits the approved archetype coalition, Primitive Coalition Contract, Final Script, Source Fidelity, Negative Space, Edge Integrity / Anti-Centroid, and Brand/Voice/Visual context when applicable.

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Every side effect is observable.
- Material changes trigger focused regression.
- Incidents quarantine only affected claims.

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. | `SRC-EXT-001` | `REFERENCE` | file:///mnt/data/Agentic Prompt Enhancer for Image Generation and.pdf | Trainable small prompt enhancers; router–rewriter–composer and downstream-output reward. |

## 5. Workflow integration

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-103 — Emit composite execution-stack fingerprints

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** Every node attempt shall record the authorized and resolved model, context, tools, retrieval indexes, runtime, precision, hardware and evaluator identities.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Emit composite execution-stack fingerprints` within feature F18.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

- Incidents quarantine only affected claims.

- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** fingerprints, sandbox denials, process receipts, canary/drift metrics, containment and restore tests, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

### FR-104 — Execute inside declared sandboxes

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** Nodes shall have explicit file, network, tool, cache, time, compute and side-effect permissions.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Execute inside declared sandboxes` within feature F18.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Every side effect is observable.
- Material changes trigger focused regression.
- Incidents quarantine only affected claims.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then nodes shall have explicit file, network, tool, cache, time, compute and side-effect permissions and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.

### FR-105 — Record observable process receipts

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** Tool calls, resource access, state mutations, validation calls, denied actions and external requests shall be independently logged.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Record observable process receipts` within feature F18.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Every side effect is observable.
- Material changes trigger focused regression.
- Incidents quarantine only affected claims.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then tool calls, resource access, state mutations, validation calls, denied actions and external requests shall be independently logged and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** fingerprints, sandbox denials, process receipts, canary/drift metrics, containment and restore tests, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D032, D033, D034, D037, D038  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-010, SRC-EXT-001


### FR-106 — Revalidate material changes

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** Changes to models, prompts, retrieval, tools, quantization, preprocessing, evaluator or runtime semantics shall trigger focused regression.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Revalidate material changes` within feature F18.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Every side effect is observable.
- Material changes trigger focused regression.
- Incidents quarantine only affected claims.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then changes to models, prompts, retrieval, tools, quantization, preprocessing, evaluator or runtime semantics shall trigger focused regression and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** fingerprints, sandbox denials, process receipts, canary/drift metrics, containment and restore tests, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D032, D033, D034, D037, D038  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-010, SRC-EXT-001


### FR-107 — Monitor production signals

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** The system shall track hard-gate failures, acceptance, candidates per result, repairs, escalations, retrieval errors, cost, latency and evaluator disagreement.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Monitor production signals` within feature F18.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Every side effect is observable.
- Material changes trigger focused regression.
- Incidents quarantine only affected claims.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then the system shall track hard-gate failures, acceptance, candidates per result, repairs, escalations, retrieval errors, cost, latency and evaluator disagreement and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** fingerprints, sandbox denials, process receipts, canary/drift metrics, containment and restore tests, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D032, D033, D034, D037, D038  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-010, SRC-EXT-001


### FR-108 — Contain and restore incidents

**Lifecycle:** `PRESERVED_AND_DEEPENED`  
**Normative requirement:** Affected claims may be quarantined, routed to a known-good fallback and restored only after regression evidence and release approval.

**Trigger and preconditions:** When a validated run, planning action, or operator request requires `Contain and restore incidents` within feature F18.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned, inspectable result or governed record that satisfies this requirement and can be consumed by the declared downstream owner.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Every side effect is observable.
- Material changes trigger focused regression.
- Incidents quarantine only affected claims.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given current authority, valid inputs, and an eligible execution binding, when this behavior runs, then affected claims may be quarantined, routed to a known-good fallback and restored only after regression evidence and release approval and the downstream consumer receives a contract-valid result.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given stale, ineligible, ambiguous, out-of-scope, or unverifiable inputs, when this behavior is requested, then no unauthorized side effect occurs and a typed blocker names the cause, owner, and next admissible action.
- **Evidence required:** fingerprints, sandbox denials, process receipts, canary/drift metrics, containment and restore tests, linked to an immutable requirement receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D032, D033, D034, D037, D038  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-010, SRC-EXT-001


## 7. Execution, model, tool, and human responsibilities

Deterministic services own mechanically decidable facts. Programmed Models or bounded Agent Programs may propose or compile behavior only within their evidence-backed claim and node-local tool grants. Independent evaluators inspect judgment dimensions. Humans own new meaning, identity interpretation, unresolved taste, operator source authority, promotion, and publication authority where assigned. The producing model or runtime cannot accept its own output.

When the feature uses a Hunter, Analyst, Composer, or Commander role, the role is an explicit workflow responsibility. It may be implemented by code, a small model, a larger model, or a human. The role name never hides the actual actor or expand its authority.

## 8. Validation and quality gates

Validation must prove both the intended result and the process that produced it. The minimum feature evidence includes fingerprints, sandbox denials, process receipts, canary/drift metrics, containment and restore tests. Mechanical tests run before expensive model or visual evaluation. Judgment evaluators are calibrated to the exact category and context. Every denial names the cause, owner, and next admissible action. Every accepted mutation emits an immutable receipt and updates only dependent state.

## 9. Risks, mitigations, and stop conditions

| Risk | Concrete consequence | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| Authority drift | A predecessor, external project, UI, model, or renderer is treated as current product authority. | Require exact source disposition, current authority validation, and product-boundary tests. |
| False completion | A synthetic URI, dry-run, unverified command, or model self-report is promoted as a real result. | Require actual files, hashes, independent validation, and artifact-class labels. |
| Over-broad automation | A model or agent gains tools, context, or authority beyond the current node. | Use JIT context, node-local tool grants, sandboxes, and explicit escalation. |
| Hidden mutation | Accepted meaning, source, program, or human preference changes without a versioned record. | Use immutable versions, typed commands, receipts, and selective invalidation. |

**Stop conditions**

- The behavior would create a second semantic or canonical state owner.
- A required source, authority, contract, primitive coalition, archetype, Final Script, runtime, evaluator, or human decision is unavailable or unverified.
- The implementation would treat migration evidence or an external project as current authority.
- The change would imply real output, production readiness, or certification beyond available evidence.

## 10. Planning and implementation handoff

This module is implementation-ready only after its FRs have one primary vertical Story owner, its Stories pass CBAR hardening, its candidate Tech Specs identify exact existing code and target paths, and Program Control issues a bounded Development Capsule. Until then, this module is a product-authority draft.

*This feature module belongs to the Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline PRD V1.1 source-first reconciliation package.*

type: prd_feature_module
product: Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline
prd_id: CA-AHP-PRD-V1.2
feature_id: F19
title: "Conscious Activations Studio Control Tower and Category Workbenches"
version: 1.2.0-draft
status: DRAFT_FOR_HUMAN_RATIFICATION
functional_requirements: "FR-109–FR-114"

# F19 — Conscious Activations Studio Control Tower and Category Workbenches

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** Operators inspect source-to-batch production, approve genuine human decisions, request corrections, and replay evidence without becoming full-time editors.

Expose one shared supervisory shell with category-native modules, canonical-program projections, autonomy modes, health, evidence, and typed commands. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The owning product is the Atomic Harness Pipeline unless an FR explicitly assigns Interview Expression, VAE, Delegation, Studio, Program Control, or an external runtime.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

**Cross-cutting Activative law:** Content activates when it gives the viewer a psychological role inside a tension. Content-bearing work inherits the approved archetype coalition, Primitive Coalition Contract, Final Script, Source Fidelity, Negative Space, Edge Integrity / Anti-Centroid, and Brand/Voice/Visual context when applicable.

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Studio read models are nonauthoritative.
- Direct manipulation uses typed command paths.
- Only assigned human authority receives actionable gates.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-AM-001` | `AMENDMENT_INPUT` | CONSCIOUS_ACTIVATIONS_STUDIO_ARCHITECTURE_AMENDMENT_V2_1(2).zip | Format 02 deferral, HumanResolutionEpisode, supervisory Studio, autonomy modes, timeline adoption, and Revision Compiler. |
| `SRC-AM-002` | `AMENDMENT_INPUT` | PA_AM_001_SEVEN_DAY_PARALLEL_PRODUCTION_ACTIVATION_V1_1(2).zip | Parallel Pipeline, temporal, static, VAE, Interview Expression, GNM, and retrieval/model-program activation lanes. |
| `SRC-INT-001` | `ADAPT` | THE_CMF_STUDIO(2).zip::05_PRD_CMF_STUDIO_INTERVIEW_FIRST.md | Interview-first source-to-asset product model and Complete Expression Session concepts. |
| `SRC-MIG-001` | `REFERENCE` | CMF_STUDIO_PREDECESSOR_MIGRATION_AUDIT_V1(1).md | Defines brownfield reuse/adapt/rewrite/archive treatment for the CMF Studio predecessor. |
| `SRC-EXT-021` | `REFERENCE_LICENSE_REVIEW` | github://openvideodev/video-editor | Multi-track timeline, drag/split/trim/snapping, interactive canvas, client-side preview/export patterns. |
| `SRC-EXT-022` | `REFERENCE_LICENSE_REVIEW` | github://lineCode/ai-video-editor | AI Copilot controlling scripts, visuals, and timeline; UI pattern only. |
| `SRC-CUR-020` | `REFERENCE` | 02_VISUAL_ASSET_EDITOR/prd/05-features/F17-steering-intelligence-cmf-okf-retrieval.md | CMF-OKF, Steering Recipes, hybrid retrieval and Minimum Complete Context. |
| `SRC-EXT-027` | `REFERENCE` | github://GoogleCloudPlatform/knowledge-catalog/okf | Portable Markdown/YAML knowledge representation with progressive disclosure and links; base for CMF-OKF profile. |
| `SRC-EXT-028` | `REFERENCE_BENCHMARK` | hf://nvidia/Nemotron-3-Embed | Candidate text/code embedding ranker after deterministic eligibility; not visual or authority layer. |
| `SRC-EXT-018` | `REFERENCE_LICENSE_REVIEW` | github://remotion-dev/remotion | React/frame source-of-truth rendering, Player, batch rendering, and editor integration. |
| `SRC-EXT-019` | `REFERENCE` | github://heygen-com/hyperframes | Deterministic HTML/CSS/GSAP motion blocks, skills, registry, Studio, and Player. |
| `SRC-EXT-026` | `REFERENCE` | github://google/GNM | Apache-2.0 parametric 3D head geometry with identity, expression, pose, gaze, and internal anatomy controls; VAE-only bounded route. |

## 5. Workflow integration

Validated upstream state → feature behavior → typed output and receipt → downstream handoff → evaluation, invalidation, and replay.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-109 — Expose source-to-batch run and graph projections

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The Studio Control Tower shall show the Canonical Interview Source Package, content-batch jobs, Harnesses, phases, Workflow Nodes, bounded roles, owners, status, blockers, costs, artifacts, source-time lineage, and exact execution evidence.

**Trigger and preconditions:** An operator opens a project, source package, campaign, or run.

**Required output or state transition:** Live read models for source, batch, run graph, artifacts, evidence, human gates, and next admissible actions.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Read models do not become authority stores.
- Synthetic/dry-run/real artifact classes are unmistakable.
- Role labels do not hide actual execution actors.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given one interview producing a short, Carousel, and SuperVisual, when the batch board opens, then the operator can trace every output to the same source package and exact source spans.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a UI fixture or stale projection that cannot prove its source state, when displayed, then it is labeled nonauthoritative and cannot drive a command.
- **Evidence required:** Read-model consistency tests, realtime event mapping, source-lineage drill-down, and projection freshness receipts.

**Governing decisions:** D005, D024, D031, D038, D046, D048, D052  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-001, SRC-AM-002, SRC-INT-001, SRC-MIG-001


### FR-110 — Provide category-native supervisory previews over canonical programs

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Static, video, interview, VAE, and knowledge/model Studio modules shall display the current canonical programs, source evidence, assets, candidates, evaluations, repairs, and allowed human actions without owning hidden production state.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A run reaches a reviewable state or an operator enters a category-native Studio.

**Required output or state transition:** Interactive projections of Composition IR, VideoEditProgram, source transcript/time map, VAE demands/results, and model/retrieval evidence.

**Authority and invariants:**
- UI state round-trips into typed commands.
- Reopening reconstructs from canonical records.
- Direct manipulation cannot bypass validation.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a video cut moved by drag, when committed, then the Studio emits the same typed ChangeRequestProgram as an equivalent natural-language request.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a timeline edit stored only in browser memory, when the page reloads, then it is not accepted and the canonical timeline remains unchanged.
- **Evidence required:** Round-trip tests, command receipts, reload/replay tests, and UI/canonical-state consistency.

**Governing decisions:** D005, D024, D031, D048, D049  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-001, SRC-MIG-001, SRC-EXT-021, SRC-EXT-022


### FR-111 — Apply Harness autonomy modes and explicit human gates

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Each campaign shall operate in AUTOPILOT, REVIEW_BEFORE_SHIP, CHECKPOINTED, or SHADOW mode, pausing only at declared human authority nodes, genuine exceptions, budget or policy changes, or unresolved taste boundaries.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A campaign is launched or a node encounters a human-owned condition.

**Required output or state transition:** An autonomy-policy binding, human-gate records, exception package, and resume decision.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Mature Harnesses target exception-only supervision.
- Humans are not asked to approve deterministic facts.
- No publication occurs beyond the mode’s authority.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given REVIEW_BEFORE_SHIP mode, when all production nodes pass, then one final acceptance is requested without intermediate pauses unless a genuine exception occurred.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given SHADOW mode, when all outputs pass evaluation, then publication remains prohibited.
- **Evidence required:** Autonomy binding, pause/resume logs, authority tests, and publication-denial receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D005, D024, D048  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-001, SRC-AM-002


### FR-112 — Inspect retrieval, Skills, recipes, Programmed Models, and exclusions

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Operators shall be able to inspect the JIT Capsule, retrieved Skills and Steering Recipes, authority filters, exclusions, contradictory evidence, model claim envelope, benchmark evidence, limitations, fallbacks, and the reason each item influenced the current decision.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A learned, retrieval-backed, or taste-bearing node is reviewed.

**Required output or state transition:** A human-readable evidence view linked to exact retrieval and model receipts.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Similarity never appears as authority.
- Protected evaluator internals remain hidden.
- Unavailable context is disclosed.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a static strategy proposal, when inspected, then the operator sees the selected Skill, two eligible recipes, one relevant negative precedent, and the exact exclusions.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a semantically similar but wrong-category recipe, when the operator inspects retrieval, then it appears only in the exclusion evidence and not the active JIT Capsule.
- **Evidence required:** Retrieval receipt, claim manifest, benchmark links, and UI evidence tests.

**Governing decisions:** D005, D024, D048  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-020, SRC-EXT-027, SRC-EXT-028, SRC-AM-002


### FR-113 — Expose runtime, provider, worker, and budget health

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The Studio shall expose preflight, compatibility, health, queue, lease, resource, cost, and failure evidence for Skia, PRETEXT, FFmpeg, Remotion, HyperFrames, VAE providers, GNM, workers, and other bound embodiments without treating their presence as production certification.

**Trigger and preconditions:** An operator inspects a binding, campaign, active worker, blocker, or incident.

**Required output or state transition:** Capability and worker health projections, budget usage, exact blocker cause, owner, and next admissible action.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Health does not imply quality certification.
- Credentials and secrets are never exposed.
- Unavailable capabilities cannot be silently emulated.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a failed Remotion worker preflight, when inspected, then the Studio shows the exact dependency/version failure and blocks only the affected nodes.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a fake provider result or synthetic URI, when health/result views load, then the artifact is clearly nonproduction and cannot satisfy completion.
- **Evidence required:** Health receipts, worker heartbeats, budget ledger, blocker records, and security tests.

**Governing decisions:** D005, D024, D038, D050  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-002, SRC-MIG-001, SRC-EXT-018, SRC-EXT-019, SRC-EXT-026


### FR-114 — Export source-to-ship audit and replay packages

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** A completed campaign shall export the source package manifest, content-batch plan, Harnesses and bindings, JIT Capsules, typed programs, HumanResolutionEpisodes, artifacts, evaluations, execution fingerprints, logs, publication evidence, and replay instructions needed to reconstruct the accepted result.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A campaign reaches accepted, rejected, canceled, shadow-complete, or published terminal state.

**Required output or state transition:** A portable audit/replay bundle with exact hashes and claim boundaries.

**Authority and invariants:**
- No secrets or absolute machine paths.
- Historical human decisions are replayed as recorded rather than regenerated.
- External missing dependencies are declared.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a published short and Carousel, when the audit package is opened elsewhere, then the source lineage and all accepted decisions can be verified even if rendering dependencies are unavailable.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given an artifact with no source or execution fingerprint, when export runs, then the bundle fails completeness validation.
- **Evidence required:** Portable bundle validation, hash manifest, secret/path scan, and clean-room replay report.

**Governing decisions:** D005, D024, D038, D044, D047  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-001, SRC-AM-002, SRC-MIG-001


## 7. Execution, model, tool, and human responsibilities

Deterministic services own mechanically decidable facts. Programmed Models or bounded Agent Programs may propose or compile behavior only within their evidence-backed claim and node-local tool grants. Independent evaluators inspect judgment dimensions. # F20 — Source-First Release 1, Expansion, and Implementation Readiness

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** The product proves one real interview-to-content-batch slice and expands only through evidence-backed boundaries.

Replace the static-only first slice with a real source-led short plus static derivative, human correction, evaluation, replay, and truthful claim states. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. ## 5. Workflow integration

Validated upstream state → feature behavior → typed output and receipt → downstream handoff → evaluation, invalidation, and replay.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-115 — Build the source-first interview-to-content-batch reference slice

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Release 1 shall admit one real Activative Interview or imported interview, produce an accepted Canonical Interview Source Package, launch a source-backed batch, render one talking-head A-roll short and one Carousel or SuperVisual from the same source, execute bounded evaluation and repair, record at least one HumanResolutionEpisode, and preserve exact source lineage.

**Trigger and preconditions:** Program Control authorizes the bounded Release 1 evidence campaign.

**Required output or state transition:** Real source package, content-batch plan, real short video, real static derivative, evaluation/repair receipts, human-resolution evidence, and audit bundle.

**Authority and invariants:**
- No fake URIs or synthetic assets count as real output.
- Talking-head A-roll remains the short’s base timeline.
- Format 02 is excluded.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given one accepted interview source, when the reference slice completes, then both outputs trace to exact source spans and pass technical, semantic, composition, and source-lineage gates.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given only a static synthetic fixture or a generated script with no interview source, when release evidence is assessed, then Release 1 remains incomplete.
- **Evidence required:** Real-file hashes, source-time maps, render/evaluation receipts, HumanResolutionEpisode, and operator acceptance.

**Governing decisions:** D039, D040, D041, D042, D043, D044, D054  
**Exact source references:** SRC-INT-001, SRC-AM-001, SRC-AM-002, SRC-EXT-017, SRC-MIG-001


### FR-116 — Require complete source-first release evidence

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The Release 1 slice shall prove source authority and identity, dual-admission correctness, Harness and binding authority, retrieval relevance, program validity, renderer correctness, independent evaluation, local repair, human resolution capture, sandbox, cancellation/replay, fallback, and truthful claim ceilings.

**Trigger and preconditions:** Release readiness is evaluated.

**Required output or state transition:** A release evidence matrix, blockers, scope claims, and readiness receipt.

**Authority and invariants:**
- One happy path cannot certify the product.
- Implementation completion is not evidence closure.
- Human participant and source authority are explicit.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given the reference slice and required negative cases, when the matrix passes, then only the bounded source-first scope may be promoted.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given missing evaluator calibration or source authority evidence, when readiness is computed, then production readiness remains false.
- **Evidence required:** Case-family reports, evaluator metrics, recovery/replay, source authority/operator source authorization evidence, and release receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D039, D040, D054  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-001, SRC-AM-002, SRC-CUR-018, SRC-CUR-019


### FR-117 — Reconcile current repository and operator-local truth before implementation

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Implementation shall not begin until public and operator-local Builder, VAE, Delegation, Studio predecessor, campaign-amendment, and source-crosswalk states are reconciled into one Program Control status without rewriting historical receipts.

**Trigger and preconditions:** The PRD or an implementation campaign seeks authorization.

**Required output or state transition:** One current status receipt, exact source hashes, resolved conflicts, and a bounded implementation allowlist.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Historical receipts remain immutable.
- Unverified local paths are not silently authoritative.
- All products consume the same current status.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given newer local terminal receipts, when verified, then Program Control publishes a superseding current status linked to both old and new evidence.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given operator-reported files that cannot be read or hashed, when reconciliation runs, then implementation remains blocked.
- **Evidence required:** Status reconciliation report, source manifests, conflict dispositions, and Program Control receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D039, D040, D054  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-003, SRC-CUR-011, SRC-STATE-001, SRC-MIG-001, SRC-MIG-002


### FR-118 — Expand one source, category, runtime, provider, or learned claim boundary at a time

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Every expansion beyond Release 1 shall declare its source-package requirements, category/profile, derivative contract, runtime or provider binding, learned claim envelope, evaluator profile, source authority scope, rollback, and scope-specific evidence.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A team proposes a new profile, derivative, runtime, provider, model claim, or source type.

**Required output or state transition:** An expansion proposal, evidence cut, compatibility manifest, and bounded authorization decision.

**Authority and invariants:**
- No automatic inheritance of certification.
- Category identities remain distinct.
- New providers do not become product authority.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a second short-video archetype, when proposed, then its source/sequence/evaluation differences and benchmark cases are explicit.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a successful Carousel recipe, when reused for a SuperVisual without category evidence, then expansion is denied.
- **Evidence required:** Expansion manifest, benchmark/evaluation plan, compatibility tests, and authorization receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D039, D040, D054  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-003, SRC-AM-001, SRC-AM-002


### FR-119 — Separate implementation, evidence closure, production readiness, and certification

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Feature code, local tests, successful real outputs, production readiness, evaluator certification, and product certification shall remain separate claim states with independent evidence and authority.

**Trigger and preconditions:** Any status, UI, report, or release process describes completion.

**Required output or state transition:** A truthful claim-state projection and maximum supported claim.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Offline implementation cannot close real evidence gates.
- Capability presence cannot confer certification.
- Synthetic and real artifacts are distinct.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a real render but no recovery evidence, when status is displayed, then it may claim a real bounded output but not production readiness.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given all unit tests pass, when a release report tries to claim certified, then claim-ceiling enforcement rejects it.
- **Evidence required:** Claim-state tests, evidence matrix, status receipts, and UI labeling checks.

**Governing decisions:** D039, D040, D054  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-003, SRC-CUR-021, SRC-MIG-001


### FR-120 — Generate a bounded PRD-to-implementation handoff

**Lifecycle:** `AMENDED_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** After human ratification, the PRD shall produce a canonical FR ledger, value-based Epics, vertical CBAR-hardened Stories, Tech Spec candidates, exact source reuse dispositions, target paths, tests, evidence gates, Development Capsules, and authority boundaries without treating the planning package as implementation authorization.

**Trigger and preconditions:** The updated PRD passes structural and authority review.

**Required output or state transition:** Planning package, traceability matrices, candidate spec inventory, source allowlists, and next authorization request.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Every FR has one primary Story owner.
- Every Story names downstream failure and proof.
- Specs read exact brownfield files before design.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given the ratified PRD, when the planning factory runs, then all requirements map to one primary Story and candidate specs identify exact source paths and boundaries.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given an unmapped requirement or duplicate primary owner, when validation runs, then the handoff fails.
- **Evidence required:** Traceability validation, Story/FR ownership report, source-crosswalk validation, and planning receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D039, D040, D054  
**Exact source references:** SRC-MIG-001, SRC-MIG-002, SRC-TREE-001, SRC-SPEC-001


## 7. Execution, model, tool, and human responsibilities

Deterministic services own mechanically decidable facts. Programmed Models or bounded Agent Programs may propose or compile behavior only within their evidence-backed claim and node-local tool grants. Independent evaluators inspect judgment dimensions. Humans own new meaning, identity interpretation, unresolved taste, operator source authority, promotion, and publication authority where assigned. The producing model or runtime cannot accept its own output.

When the feature uses a Hunter, Analyst, Composer, or Commander role, the role is an explicit workflow responsibility. It may be implemented by code, a small model, a larger model, or a human. The role name never hides the actual actor or expand its authority.

## 8. Validation and quality gates

Validation must prove both the intended result and the process that produced it. The minimum feature evidence includes real source/output hashes, release case matrix, source authority, retrieval, runtime, evaluation, recovery, human resolution, and claim receipts. Mechanical tests run before expensive model or visual evaluation. Judgment evaluators are calibrated to the exact category and context. Every denial names the cause, owner, and next admissible action. Every accepted mutation emits an immutable receipt and updates only dependent state.

## 9. Risks, mitigations, and stop conditions

| Risk | Concrete consequence | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| Authority drift | A predecessor, external project, UI, model, or renderer is treated as current product authority. | Require exact source disposition, current authority validation, and product-boundary tests. |
| False completion | A synthetic URI, dry-run, unverified command, or model self-report is promoted as a real result. | Require actual files, hashes, independent validation, and artifact-class labels. |
| Over-broad automation | A model or agent gains tools, context, or authority beyond the current node. | Use JIT context, node-local tool grants, sandboxes, and explicit escalation. |
| Hidden mutation | Accepted meaning, source, program, or human preference changes without a versioned record. | Use immutable versions, typed commands, receipts, and selective invalidation. |

**Stop conditions**

- The behavior would create a second semantic or canonical state owner.
- A required source, authority, contract, primitive coalition, archetype, Final Script, runtime, evaluator, or human decision is unavailable or unverified.
- The implementation would treat migration evidence or an external project as current authority.
- The change would imply real output, production readiness, or certification beyond available evidence.

## 10. Planning and implementation handoff

This module is implementation-ready only after its FRs have one primary vertical Story owner, its Stories pass CBAR hardening, its candidate Tech Specs identify exact existing code and target paths, and Program Control issues a bounded Development Capsule. Until then, this module is a product-authority draft.

*This feature module belongs to the Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline PRD V1.1 source-first reconciliation package.*
