# F26 — Operator Revision Compiler and Human Resolution Programming Material

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** Natural-language and direct-manipulation corrections become minimal typed changes, selective reruns, and reusable evidence.

Compile operator intent into bounded tool programs, validate authority/minimality, evaluate results, and capture every meaningful decision. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

Studio captures intent; Pipeline validates and executes; Knowledge/Model systems consume eligible episodes.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

**Cross-cutting Activative law:** Content activates when it gives the viewer a psychological role inside a tension. Content-bearing work inherits the approved archetype coalition, Primitive Coalition Contract, Final Script, Source Fidelity, Negative Space, Edge Integrity / Anti-Centroid, and Brand/Voice/Visual context when applicable.

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- No direct UI mutation bypasses the command path.
- Prior accepted state remains until replacement passes.
- Learning is scoped and offline-promoted.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-AM-001` | `AMENDMENT_INPUT` | CONSCIOUS_ACTIVATIONS_STUDIO_ARCHITECTURE_AMENDMENT_V2_1(2).zip | Format 02 deferral, HumanResolutionEpisode, supervisory Studio, autonomy modes, timeline adoption, and Revision Compiler. |
| `SRC-AM-002` | `AMENDMENT_INPUT` | PA_AM_001_SEVEN_DAY_PARALLEL_PRODUCTION_ACTIVATION_V1_1(2).zip | Parallel Pipeline, temporal, static, VAE, Interview Expression, GNM, and retrieval/model-program activation lanes. |
| `SRC-EXT-021` | `REFERENCE_LICENSE_REVIEW` | github://openvideodev/video-editor | Multi-track timeline, drag/split/trim/snapping, interactive canvas, client-side preview/export patterns. |
| `SRC-EXT-022` | `REFERENCE_LICENSE_REVIEW` | github://lineCode/ai-video-editor | AI Copilot controlling scripts, visuals, and timeline; UI pattern only. |
| `SRC-CUR-010` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/src/cmf_builder/workflow/actor_explicit_contracts.py | Execution-free Workflow Node, edge, authority and validation contracts. |
| `SRC-CUR-019` | `REFERENCE` | 02_VISUAL_ASSET_EDITOR/prd/05-features/F15-repair-invalidation-reruns.md | Typed visual repair and bounded reruns. |
| `SRC-EXT-017` | `REFERENCE` | github://browser-use/video-use | Packed phrase transcript, word-boundary EDL, FFmpeg correctness, rendered cut evaluation, bounded repair, and project memory. |
| `SRC-CUR-020` | `REFERENCE` | 02_VISUAL_ASSET_EDITOR/prd/05-features/F17-steering-intelligence-cmf-okf-retrieval.md | CMF-OKF, Steering Recipes, hybrid retrieval and Minimum Complete Context. |

## 5. Workflow integration

Operator language or direct manipulation → ChangeRequestProgram → authority/minimality validation → selective rerun → evaluation → commit/reject → HumanResolutionEpisode.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-151 — Compile natural-language operator revisions into typed change programs

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** A Revision Compiler Programmed Model or eligible general fallback shall translate an authorized operator request, current state, target objects, Harness, JIT context, allowed tool registry, and evaluation into the smallest typed ChangeRequestProgram or an explicit clarification/escalation.

**Trigger and preconditions:** An operator submits a revision in a category Studio or review queue.

**Required output or state transition:** A structured interpretation, exact operations, preconditions, invariants, affected nodes, validation plan, confidence, and escalation state.

**Authority and invariants:**
- The compiler proposes commands; deterministic authority validation decides admission.
- Unclear requests may ask one targeted question.
- No unrestricted tool access.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given 'let the reaction breathe half a second longer and lower the caption,' when context is sufficient, then the compiler emits exact temporal and layout operations with affected nodes.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given 'make it better' with multiple plausible meanings, when confidence is insufficient, then it requests clarification rather than guessing.
- **Evidence required:** Tool-call schema tests, human request benchmark, argument accuracy, over-edit rate, and interpretation receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D047, D049  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-001, SRC-AM-002


### FR-152 — Convert direct manipulation into the same typed command path

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Dragging, trimming, splitting, resizing, cropping, reordering, selecting a candidate, or changing a parameter in the Studio shall produce the same canonical ChangeRequestProgram and validation path as an equivalent language request.

**Trigger and preconditions:** An operator performs a direct manipulation and attempts to commit it.

**Required output or state transition:** A typed command/delta linked to before-state, target, user authority, and preview.

**Authority and invariants:**
- The UI cannot mutate accepted state directly.
- Undo and replay are command-based.
- Equivalent actions have equivalent evidence.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a twelve-frame clip move, when committed, then the canonical program changes through a validated move operation and the same episode schema used for text revisions.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given an unsupported canvas drag outside permitted geometry tolerance, when committed, then the command is rejected or converted into an amendment proposal.
- **Evidence required:** UI-to-command round-trip tests, undo/replay, before/after hashes, and HumanResolutionEpisode.

**Governing decisions:** D047, D049  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-001, SRC-EXT-021, SRC-EXT-022


### FR-153 — Validate revision authority, scope, and minimality before execution

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Every ChangeRequestProgram shall pass schema, current-state identity, authority, tool grant, Transformation Contract, source truth, geometry/timing, budget, and minimal-change validation before preview or execution.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A compiled or manually constructed change program is submitted.

**Required output or state transition:** An admitted dry-run/preview plan or typed denial with exact cause and next action.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Valid existing relationships are preserved.
- Out-of-scope meaning changes require the owning authority.
- Stale-state commands cannot commit.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a caption shift within safe bounds, when validated, then it may preview without invalidating A-roll selection.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a stale command targeting a superseded composition version, when validation runs, then it is denied.
- **Evidence required:** Schema/authority tests, stale-state race tests, minimal-diff analysis, and admission receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D047, D049  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-010, SRC-AM-001


### FR-154 — Rerun only affected work and independently evaluate the result

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** An accepted revision shall invalidate only directly changed objects and dependent nodes, reuse unaffected checkpoints and assets, render an appropriate preview, run required deterministic and independent evaluations, and either commit, reject, or escalate.

**Trigger and preconditions:** Revision validation succeeds.

**Required output or state transition:** A selective rerun plan, new artifacts, evaluation, commit/reject state, and dependency updates.

**Authority and invariants:**
- No full-batch rerun without dependency evidence.
- Rejected preview leaves prior accepted state intact.
- Repair limits prevent loops.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a SuperVisual text-size change, when executed, then only text layout, render, and dependent evaluation rerun.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a local edit that causes a new wrong-reading failure, when evaluated, then it is rejected and the prior accepted version remains current.
- **Evidence required:** Checkpoint reuse report, invalidation graph, render diffs, evaluation, and state transaction receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D047, D049  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-019, SRC-AM-001, SRC-EXT-017


### FR-155 — Emit a HumanResolutionEpisode for every meaningful human decision

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Every approval, rejection, candidate selection, revision, manual change, tool override, escalation resolution, taste explanation, and publication decision shall emit an immutable HumanResolutionEpisode linked to the exact before/after state, operations, evidence, authority, and applicability scope.

**Trigger and preconditions:** An authorized human decision commits.

**Required output or state transition:** A complete HumanResolutionEpisode and automatic retrieval/programming-material disposition.

**Authority and invariants:**
- No meaningful decision is stored only as UI telemetry.
- Scope defaults to narrow.
- Human rationale may remain optional but absence is explicit.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given an operator rejects candidate A and selects B because A feels too polished, when committed, then the pair and reason are captured as scoped preference evidence.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given an anonymous button click with no run or authority context, when persistence runs, then it cannot become a resolution episode.
- **Evidence required:** Episode completeness validation, exact change/tool links, scope tests, and indexing receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D047  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-001


### FR-156 — Use human-resolution evidence for governed retrieval and Programmed Model improvement

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Eligible HumanResolutionEpisodes shall become immediately retrievable precedents and may later produce supervised examples, preference pairs, hard negatives, repair trajectories, Steering Recipe evidence, or model-training candidates through offline operator-authorized dataset, shadow, evaluation, and promotion gates.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A HumanResolutionEpisode closes and attribution completes.

**Required output or state transition:** Retrieval index entry, candidate learning dispositions, and later promotion artifacts where authorized.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Immediate retrieval does not mean universal applicability.
- Training eligibility follows operator-declared source authority.
- No live weight mutation.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given repeated accepted video corrections in one profile, when a future Revision Compiler is evaluated, then held-out episodes can test whether it predicts the same minimal operations.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given one idiosyncratic workspace preference, when global recipe promotion is requested, then evidence scope blocks it.
- **Evidence required:** Indexing tests, dataset eligibility, shadow replay, claim benchmark, and promotion receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D047  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-001, SRC-CUR-020


## 7. Execution, model, tool, and human responsibilities

Deterministic services own mechanically decidable facts. Programmed Models or bounded Agent Programs may propose or compile behavior only within their evidence-backed claim and node-local tool grants. Independent evaluators inspect judgment dimensions. Humans own new meaning, identity interpretation, unresolved taste, operator source authority, promotion, and publication authority where assigned. The producing model or runtime cannot accept its own output.

When the feature uses a Hunter, Analyst, Composer, or Commander role, the role is an explicit workflow responsibility. It may be implemented by code, a small model, a larger model, or a human. The role name never hides the actual actor or expand its authority.

## 8. Validation and quality gates

Validation must prove both the intended result and the process that produced it. The minimum feature evidence includes revision benchmark, UI-command round-trip, validation, selective rerun, HumanResolutionEpisode, and shadow/promotion. Mechanical tests run before expensive model or visual evaluation. Judgment evaluators are calibrated to the exact category and context. Every denial names the cause, owner, and next admissible action. Every accepted mutation emits an immutable receipt and updates only dependent state.

## 9. Risks, mitigations, and stop conditions

| Risk | Concrete consequence | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| Authority drift | A predecessor, external project, UI, model, or renderer is treated as current product authority. | Require exact source disposition, current authority validation, and product-boundary tests. |
| False completion | A synthetic URI, dry-run, unverified command, or model self-report is promoted as a real result. | Require actual files, hashes, independent validation, and artifact-class labels. |
| Over-broad automation | A model or agent gains tools, context, or authority beyond the current node. | Use JIT context, node-local tool grants, sandboxes, and explicit escalation. |
| Hidden mutation | Accepted meaning, source, program, or human preference changes without a versioned record. | Use immutable versions, typed commands, receipts, and selective invalidation. |

**Stop conditions**

- The behavior would create a second semantic or canonical state owner.
- A required source, authority, contract, primitive coalition, archetype, Final Script, runtime, evaluator, or human decision is unavailable or unverified.
- The implementation would treat migration evidence or an external project as current authority.
- The change would imply real output, production readiness, or certification beyond available evidence.

## 10. Planning and implementation handoff

This module is implementation-ready only after its FRs have one primary vertical Story owner, its Stories pass CBAR hardening, its candidate Tech Specs identify exact existing code and target paths, and Program Control issues a bounded Development Capsule. Until then, this module is a product-authority draft.

*This feature module belongs to the Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline PRD V1.1 source-first reconciliation package.*

# F27 — Studio Campaign Autonomy and Category-Native Supervision

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** Operators order, supervise, correct, and ship campaigns through one Studio shell while Atomic Harnesses conduct the work.

Launch source-backed batches, route category modules, enforce autonomy modes, package exceptions, and govern delivery/publication. This feature exists to convert doctrine and source evidence into behavior that can be implemented, tested, denied, replayed, and audited. It does not grant implementation, provider, model-training, publication, production, or certification authority by itself.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

Studio owns projections and typed operator commands; canonical state remains in product services.

The feature must preserve the current product topology. Builder supplies the immutable Atomic Harness; Pipeline executes its declared nodes; Interview Expression owns source expression preparation and approval; VAE owns visual production; Delegation owns cross-product envelopes; Studio projects state and emits typed operator commands; Program Control owns cross-product authority and release truth. External renderers and models are embodiments, not sources of meaning.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

**Cross-cutting Activative law:** Content activates when it gives the viewer a psychological role inside a tension. Content-bearing work inherits the approved archetype coalition, Primitive Coalition Contract, Final Script, Source Fidelity, Negative Space, Edge Integrity / Anti-Centroid, and Brand/Voice/Visual context when applicable.

The feature consumes current, versioned upstream records and emits typed outputs that remain linked to the active Harness, source package where applicable, Workflow Node, JIT Capsule, execution binding, evaluator, and receipt. Canonical records use stable serialization and immutable identities. A UI projection, model response, provider job, renderer workspace, or local cache cannot become accepted product state until its contract and authority gates pass.

Core invariants for this feature are:

- Studio modules do not own canonical state.
- SHADOW cannot publish.
- Human gates occur only at declared authority boundaries.

## 4. Brownfield and external capability treatment

The implementation begins from exact current and predecessor evidence. The table below identifies the most relevant source records. `REUSE` or `ADAPT` permits bounded implementation reuse after namespace, authority, license, dependency, and behavior review; it never imports historical product meaning automatically.

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-AM-001` | `AMENDMENT_INPUT` | CONSCIOUS_ACTIVATIONS_STUDIO_ARCHITECTURE_AMENDMENT_V2_1(2).zip | Format 02 deferral, HumanResolutionEpisode, supervisory Studio, autonomy modes, timeline adoption, and Revision Compiler. |
| `SRC-AM-002` | `AMENDMENT_INPUT` | PA_AM_001_SEVEN_DAY_PARALLEL_PRODUCTION_ACTIVATION_V1_1(2).zip | Parallel Pipeline, temporal, static, VAE, Interview Expression, GNM, and retrieval/model-program activation lanes. |
| `SRC-INT-001` | `ADAPT` | THE_CMF_STUDIO(2).zip::05_PRD_CMF_STUDIO_INTERVIEW_FIRST.md | Interview-first source-to-asset product model and Complete Expression Session concepts. |
| `SRC-MIG-001` | `REFERENCE` | CMF_STUDIO_PREDECESSOR_MIGRATION_AUDIT_V1(1).md | Defines brownfield reuse/adapt/rewrite/archive treatment for the CMF Studio predecessor. |
| `SRC-CUR-004` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/src/cmf_builder/domain/atomic_harness_definition.py | Canonical AtomicHarnessDefinition structure and execution-free status. |
| `SRC-CUR-010` | `REFERENCE` | 01_ATOMIC_HARNESS_BUILDER/src/cmf_builder/workflow/actor_explicit_contracts.py | Execution-free Workflow Node, edge, authority and validation contracts. |

## 5. Workflow integration

Campaign order → source/Harness/binding validation → autonomy mode → execution projections → exception review → correction → ship/export/publish.

Every handoff is typed. A downstream node begins only after the producer output passes the declared contract and evidence gates. Failures are attributed to source, knowledge, retrieval, Skill, recipe, Programmed Model, tool, runtime, product, evaluator, or human-policy layers before repair or escalation.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-157 — Launch campaigns from source packages or Asset Package Specs

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The Studio shall let an authorized operator select a workspace/project, inspect or complete a Canonical Interview Source Package, choose target outputs and Harnesses, set seed/taste direction, budget, deadline, autonomy mode, and launch a governed content batch.

**Trigger and preconditions:** An operator wants to produce a batch from an interview source.

**Required output or state transition:** A Campaign Order, validated batch plan, bindings, budget reservation, and launch receipt.

**Authority and invariants:**
- The Studio cannot invent missing Harnesses.
- Source/source authority eligibility precedes launch.
- Order data does not bypass product contracts.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given an imported interview source, when the operator selects one short and one Carousel, then the Studio validates both Harnesses and launches one coordinated batch.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a requested Format 02 output before activation, when the order is validated, then that job is blocked and the rest may proceed if eligible.
- **Evidence required:** Order schema, source/Harness validation, budget checks, autonomy binding, and launch receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D046, D048  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-001, SRC-AM-002, SRC-INT-001


### FR-158 — Operate one shared Studio shell with category-native modules

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The product shall provide one shared workspace, project, campaign, run, review, evidence, artifact, worker, provider, budget, and publishing shell while registering Interview Expression, Video Production, Static Composition, Visual Asset, and Knowledge/Programmed Model modules behind current product boundaries.

**Trigger and preconditions:** An operator navigates across source, production, review, or learning work.

**Required output or state transition:** Shared shell routes and category-module read/action contracts.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Modules do not duplicate canonical state or authority.
- A module loads only relevant tools and evidence.
- Future Character Performance remains deferred.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a source-led batch, when the operator moves from Interview to Video to Static review, then all modules display the same source and campaign identities.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a module attempting to own VAE state locally, when architecture tests run, then the duplication is rejected.
- **Evidence required:** Route/read-model integration tests, shared identity consistency, product-boundary tests, and accessibility review.

**Governing decisions:** D048  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-001, SRC-MIG-001


### FR-159 — Support AUTOPILOT, REVIEW_BEFORE_SHIP, CHECKPOINTED, and SHADOW modes

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Campaign and Harness bindings shall declare one autonomy mode, allowed human gates, publication authority, exception policy, and mode changes, with mature Harnesses targeting AUTOPILOT or REVIEW_BEFORE_SHIP rather than continuous manual editing.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A campaign is configured or its governance mode changes.

**Required output or state transition:** A versioned autonomy policy and mode-specific workflow behavior.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Mode changes are authorized and receipted.
- SHADOW never publishes.
- AUTOPILOT still escalates genuine authority or operator-owned creative conflicts.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given CHECKPOINTED mode, when a declared creative gate is reached, then the Studio pauses with a complete decision package.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given AUTOPILOT mode and a deterministic validation pass, when no human-owned conflict exists, then the system does not ask for approval.
- **Evidence required:** Mode transition tests, gate/publish enforcement, exception simulations, and receipts.

**Governing decisions:** D048  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-001, SRC-AM-002


### FR-160 — Provide exception-only review packages and attributable decisions

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** When human attention is required, the Studio shall present the exact issue, source and current state, candidates or alternatives, evaluator evidence, authority owner, costs and downstream effects, and permitted actions without forcing the operator to inspect raw logs or rebuild the work.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A human gate, taste boundary, policy conflict, budget change, or unrecoverable exception occurs.

**Required output or state transition:** A structured ReviewPackage and subsequent HumanResolutionEpisode.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Only assigned authority sees actionable decisions.
- Deterministic facts are not disguised as creative choices.
- Unavailable evidence is disclosed.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given two valid composition candidates with unresolved taste, when review opens, then the operator sees their source lineage, differences, evaluations, and expected downstream effects.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a worker crash with an automatic retry policy, when no human action is needed, then it remains an operational incident rather than a creative review.
- **Evidence required:** Review completeness tests, role/permission checks, decision receipts, and operator usability evidence.

**Governing decisions:** D048, D052  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-001, SRC-AM-002


### FR-161 — Ship, export, or publish only under explicit authority and evidence

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** The Studio shall permit final acceptance, export, scheduling, or publication only when the derivative and campaign satisfy required technical, semantic, source authority, evaluation, lineage, and autonomy-mode gates, and shall record the human or policy authority responsible.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A derivative or batch is proposed for delivery or publication.

**Required output or state transition:** A publish/export command, delivery artifacts, metadata, signed URLs or integrations, usage records, and publication receipt.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Review-before-ship requires final acceptance.
- Source authority and revocation are rechecked at publish time.
- Publication does not imply certification.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a passed short in REVIEW_BEFORE_SHIP mode, when the operator approves, then the final artifact and source/evidence bundle are exported and the decision is captured.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a passed SHADOW artifact, when publish is requested, then the command is denied.
- **Evidence required:** Delivery-profile validation, source-authority checks, mode/authority tests, artifact hashes, and publication receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D048, D054  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-001, SRC-AM-002


### FR-162 — Route each Harness to the correct supervisory surfaces and live read models

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_1`  
**Normative requirement:** Every Atomic Harness or derivative job shall declare its primary and supporting Studio surfaces, operator-entry policy, visible evidence, permitted commands, and realtime projections without allowing the Studio plugin to change Harness meaning or runtime ownership.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A Harness is imported, bound, or launched.

**Required output or state transition:** A StudioSurfaceBinding and validated module/read-model/action configuration.

**Authority and invariants:**
- UI plugins are nonauthoritative projections.
- Unsupported surfaces cannot infer tools or state.
- Module version changes are compatibility-tested.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a short-video Harness, when imported, then Video Production is primary and Visual Asset and Knowledge/Model modules are supporting surfaces with bounded commands.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a plugin that exposes an ungranted provider action, when binding validation runs, then the plugin/action is rejected.
- **Evidence required:** Surface-binding schema, permission/action tests, realtime projection tests, and compatibility receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D048, D049  
**Exact source references:** SRC-AM-001, SRC-CUR-004, SRC-CUR-010


## 7. Execution, model, tool, and human responsibilities

prd_id: CA-AHP-PRD-V1.2

title: "Activative Psychological Role, Archetype Coalition, and Final Script Authority"

# F28 — Activative Psychological Role, Archetype Coalition, and Final Script Authority

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** Every derivative gives the viewer a clear psychological role inside a source-backed tension and reaches composition through an approved archetype-coalition Final Script.

This feature restores archetypes as execution-bearing psychological geometries and makes the Final Script the mandatory bridge between expression and composition.

The controlling Activative law is: **Content activates when it gives the viewer a psychological role inside a tension.** This feature must preserve that law from source interpretation through script, composition, render, evaluation, and repair.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The Atomic Harness Pipeline compiles and executes this behavior. Interview Expression supplies authenticated expression material. Builder supplies the category-native Harness. Studio supplies operator commands and approval. VAE supplies visual ingredients. None of these products may silently replace the approved archetype coalition, Primitive Coalition Contract, Final Script, or Activative Intelligence contracts.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

Core invariants:
- Every derivative declares a psychological role inside a tension.
- Matrix of Edging precedes archetype routing.
- Guest Voice DNA governs non-verbatim text.
- Final Script approval precedes every composition.

The feature emits immutable, versioned objects linked to source package, archetype route, Primitive Coalition Contract, Brand Context Version where applicable, Final Script, composition program, rendered result, and evaluation receipts.

## 4. Brownfield and doctrine-source treatment

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-DOCT-001` | `ADAPT` | sources/MATRIX_OF_EDGING.md | Force selection, coalition signatures, edge products, and anti-centroid law. |
| `SRC-DOCT-002` | `ADAPT` | sources/CCP_ARCHETYPE_SYSTEM_MIGRATION_PROPOSITION.md | Archetype and derivative route system. |
| `SRC-DOCT-003` | `ADAPT` | sources/CCP_CMF_BRAND_GENESIS_AND_MICRO_SEMIOTIC_PIPELINE_V3.md | Brand Context Version, Voice DNA, Visual DNA, and Negative Space. |
| `SRC-DOCT-005` | `ADAPT` | sources/CCV_COMBINATORIAL_CONTROLLED_VARIATION.md | Controlled variation and coalition composition. |
| `SRC-DOCT-006` | `ADAPT` | sources/RSCS_RECURSIVE_SIGNAL_COMPRESSION_SYSTEMS.md | Signal saturation, collision, compression, evaluation, and recursion. |
| `SRC-DOCT-009` | `ADAPT` | sources/PRIMITIVE_COALITION_CONTRACT.py | Brownfield typed coalition and evaluation objects. |

These sources are migration and doctrine evidence. Their concepts must be reconciled into current contracts rather than copied as hidden runtime authority.

## 5. Workflow integration

Source expression → Matrix of Edging → primitive candidates → candidate survival → Primitive Coalition Contract → coalition signature → edge product → archetype coalition → Guest Voice DNA Final Script → composition program → runtime embodiment → Primitive Evaluation Receipt and Activative evaluation → selective repair.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-163 — Declare the viewer psychological role inside a named tension

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_2`  
**Normative requirement:** Every derivative job shall declare the psychological role offered to the viewer, the meaningful tension that makes the role available, the intended movement through that tension, and the evidence connecting the tension to the source.

**Trigger and preconditions:** An Expression Moment or source-backed premise is proposed for derivative routing.

**Required output or state transition:** A PsychologicalRoleInTension contract attached to the archetype-routing decision.

**Authority and invariants:**
- The role is specific enough to evaluate.
- The tension comes from source and Matrix of Edging evidence.
- A topic or emotion label alone is insufficient.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given an Expression Moment about inherited silence, when routed, then the contract names the viewer role, such as witness, recognizer, challenger, or participant, and the tension the viewer enters.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a generic “inspire the audience” intention, when validation runs, then routing is blocked because no psychological role or live tension is declared.
- **Evidence required:** Source spans, Matrix of Edging trace, role/tension evaluation, and operator approval receipt.

**Governing decisions:** D055, D056  
**Exact source references:** SRC-DOCT-001, SRC-INT-002, SRC-INT-003

### FR-164 — Compile broad signal, coalition signature, and Edge Product through Matrix of Edging

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_2`  
**Normative requirement:** The system shall distinguish pre-expression broad primary signal from post-expression Edge Product formation and shall compile surviving primitive candidates into one measurable Coalition Signature.

**Trigger and preconditions:** Source expression is accepted and an archetype route is requested.

**Required output or state transition:** A MatrixOfEdgingResult containing broad signal lineage, candidate survival, coalition signature, Edge Product, and routeability.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Primitives are not edges.
- Unsupported cleverness does not survive.
- Coalition fatality remains visible.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a truth-rich source answer, when the Matrix pass runs, then broad pressure, surviving primitive candidates, coalition geometry, and the emergent Edge Product remain separately inspectable.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given an Edge Product invented directly from a topic label without primitive survival, when validation runs, then it is rejected.
- **Evidence required:** Candidate survival scores, coalition geometry, fatality cases, and routeability receipts.

**Governing decisions:** D055, D058, D066  
**Exact source references:** SRC-DOCT-001, SRC-DOCT-006, SRC-DOCT-009

### FR-165 — Compile an archetype coalition for every derivative

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_2`  
**Normative requirement:** Each derivative shall bind a primary archetype, supporting archetype functions, asset-derivative route, category grammar, psychological geometry, and tension progression as one versioned ArchetypeCoalitionContract.

**Trigger and preconditions:** An Edge Product and content-batch job are accepted.

**Required output or state transition:** An ArchetypeCoalitionContract eligible for script compilation.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Archetype is a psychological geometry, not a theme label.
- Supporting archetypes cannot blur the primary role.
- Category and substrate remain explicit.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given one Edge Product, when a Carousel and short-video route are created, then each receives a category-native archetype coalition sharing source force without sharing a flattened template.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given three attractive archetype labels with no primary geometry or sequence law, when validation runs, then the coalition is rejected.
- **Evidence required:** Archetype registry trace, coalition compatibility, category crosswalk, and CBAR audit.

**Governing decisions:** D055, D057, D066  
**Exact source references:** SRC-DOCT-002, SRC-DOCT-005, SRC-INT-003

### FR-166 — Compile text-bearing content through Guest Voice DNA

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_2`  
**Normative requirement:** JIT Skill script writers and Composers shall write or rewrite non-verbatim text through the active Guest Voice DNA, source evidence, Edge Product, archetype coalition, and Distillation Layers; verbatim quotations shall remain marked as verbatim.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A derivative needs a headline, claim, slide copy, caption, overlay, voiceover, or animation line.

**Required output or state transition:** A VoiceDNAConstrainedScriptDraft with source and transformation lineage.

**Authority and invariants:**
- No anonymous generic brand voice.
- Rewriting preserves source truth and guest cadence.
- Verbatim and rewritten language are distinguishable.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a dense interview answer, when Carousel copy is compiled, then the slides sound like the guest while using category-native compression rather than copying raw transcript mechanically.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given polished copy that could belong to any creator, when Voice DNA evaluation runs, then the draft is rejected or repaired.
- **Evidence required:** Voice DNA version, source-span crosswalk, distillation trace, contrastive examples, and VoiceContinuity evaluation.

**Governing decisions:** D060, D061, D066  
**Exact source references:** SRC-DOCT-002, SRC-DOCT-003, SRC-DOCT-006

### FR-167 — Approve one archetype-coalition Final Script before composition

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_2`  
**Normative requirement:** No Composition IR, VideoEditProgram, animation scene program, visual generation demand, or renderer workspace may be compiled until one versioned Final Script passes source fidelity, Voice DNA, archetype, primitive, Activative, and operator approval gates.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A script draft is proposed as the content substrate for a derivative.

**Required output or state transition:** An approved FinalScript record or a typed repair request.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Composition cannot conceal an unresolved script.
- Approval pins the exact source and coalition versions.
- Later revisions create a new script version.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a source-led short, when the Final Script is approved, then selected source words, overlay copy, scene roles, animation opportunities, and primitive obligations are fixed before timeline composition.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a renderer-ready layout with no approved Final Script, when execution is requested, then composition is blocked.
- **Evidence required:** Final Script review, source-fidelity evaluation, primitive receipt, archetype receipt, and operator decision.

**Governing decisions:** D057, D060, D062  
**Exact source references:** SRC-DOCT-002, SRC-DOCT-004, SRC-INT-001

### FR-168 — Preserve role, tension, coalition, and Final Script lineage through every embodiment

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_2`  
**Normative requirement:** Every content-bearing object and rendered artifact shall link to the PsychologicalRoleInTension contract, Matrix result, Primitive Coalition Contract, Archetype Coalition Contract, Final Script, source spans, and transformation history.

**Trigger and preconditions:** Any downstream composition, generation, edit, repair, or export is created.

**Required output or state transition:** Complete doctrine-to-artifact lineage and invalidation edges.

**Authority and invariants:**
- A renderer cannot erase upstream reason.
- A repair cannot change the role or tension silently.
- Cross-format reuse retains the originating coalition.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given one animation scene reused as video B-roll and on a Carousel slide, when audited, then both uses resolve to the same source, Edge Product, primitive coalition, archetype coalition, and Final Script version.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given an asset copied into another derivative without coalition lineage, when validation runs, then the use is rejected.
- **Evidence required:** Lineage graph, selective invalidation tests, cross-format reuse receipts, and replay proof.

**Governing decisions:** D044, D057, D067  
**Exact source references:** SRC-DOCT-001, SRC-DOCT-002, SRC-DOCT-009


## 7. Execution, model, tool, and human responsibilities

JIT Skill writers and Composers may draft and rewrite only inside the active Voice DNA, archetype, primitive, and source contracts. Programmed Models are bounded compilers or evaluators, not sources of doctrine. The operator approves the Final Script and any new creative boundary. Renderers execute composition programs and cannot invent the recipe.

## 8. Validation and quality gates

Validation must prove source pressure, role clarity, Voice DNA, archetype geometry, primitive coalition, and Final Script integrity. Primitive coverage, misuse, coalition fatality, source fidelity, psychological-role clarity, edge integrity, negative-space integrity, Voice DNA, Visual DNA, category grammar, and the active Activative Intelligence contracts are separate evaluation dimensions.

## 9. Risks, mitigations, and stop conditions

| Risk | Concrete consequence | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| Centroid flattening | The result is polished but carries no live tension or psychological role. | Enforce Matrix of Edging, coalition signature, Edge Product, CCV variation, and anti-centroid evaluation. |
| Primitive tokenism | Primitive IDs are attached after the creative decision rather than building it. | Require Primitive Bindings and Coalition Contract before Final Script and composition. |
| Archetype decoration | An archetype label is applied without its psychological geometry or sequence obligations. | Require an archetype coalition contract and approved Final Script. |
| Renderer-led meaning | The runtime chooses layout, motion, or imagery without the coalition recipe. | Renderer adapters consume only typed composition programs. |

**Stop conditions**

- No approved psychological role inside a named tension.
- No current Primitive Coalition Contract or archetype coalition.
- No approved Final Script before composition.
- Primitive misuse or coalition fatality exceeds the declared threshold.
- The output collapses source specificity, edge integrity, Voice DNA, Visual DNA, or category grammar.

## 10. Planning and implementation handoff

This module becomes implementation-ready only after its FRs have primary vertical Story ownership, CBAR hardening has loaded the mapped Primitive Families and misuse modes, candidate Tech Specs identify exact brownfield contracts and tests, and a bounded Development Capsule is issued.

*This feature module belongs to the Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline PRD V1.2 primitive- and archetype-centered reconciliation package.*

# F29 — Primitive-First Coalition Composition and Evaluation

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** Primitive Families and Bindings build the real creative recipe, coalitions organize force, and evaluations measure primitive coverage, misuse, fatality, and Edge Product survival.

This feature makes primitives upstream recipe builders rather than decorative tags and positions Steering Recipes as evidence-backed execution strategies derived from the coalition.

The controlling Activative law is: **Content activates when it gives the viewer a psychological role inside a tension.** This feature must preserve that law from source interpretation through script, composition, render, evaluation, and repair.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The Atomic Harness Pipeline compiles and executes this behavior. Interview Expression supplies authenticated expression material. Builder supplies the category-native Harness. Studio supplies operator commands and approval. VAE supplies visual ingredients. None of these products may silently replace the approved archetype coalition, Primitive Coalition Contract, Final Script, or Activative Intelligence contracts.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

Core invariants:
- Meaning and Experience Primitive planes remain distinct.
- Primitive Bindings precede coalition and recipe selection.
- Coalition Signature and Edge Product are measurable objects.
- Primitive Evaluation Receipts are mandatory for content-bearing outputs.

The feature emits immutable, versioned objects linked to source package, archetype route, Primitive Coalition Contract, Brand Context Version where applicable, Final Script, composition program, rendered result, and evaluation receipts.

## 4. Brownfield and doctrine-source treatment

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-DOCT-001` | `ADAPT` | sources/MATRIX_OF_EDGING.md | Force selection, coalition signatures, edge products, and anti-centroid law. |
| `SRC-DOCT-002` | `ADAPT` | sources/CCP_ARCHETYPE_SYSTEM_MIGRATION_PROPOSITION.md | Archetype and derivative route system. |
| `SRC-DOCT-003` | `ADAPT` | sources/CCP_CMF_BRAND_GENESIS_AND_MICRO_SEMIOTIC_PIPELINE_V3.md | Brand Context Version, Voice DNA, Visual DNA, and Negative Space. |
| `SRC-DOCT-005` | `ADAPT` | sources/CCV_COMBINATORIAL_CONTROLLED_VARIATION.md | Controlled variation and coalition composition. |
| `SRC-DOCT-006` | `ADAPT` | sources/RSCS_RECURSIVE_SIGNAL_COMPRESSION_SYSTEMS.md | Signal saturation, collision, compression, evaluation, and recursion. |
| `SRC-DOCT-009` | `ADAPT` | sources/PRIMITIVE_COALITION_CONTRACT.py | Brownfield typed coalition and evaluation objects. |

These sources are migration and doctrine evidence. Their concepts must be reconciled into current contracts rather than copied as hidden runtime authority.

## 5. Workflow integration

Source expression → Matrix of Edging → primitive candidates → candidate survival → Primitive Coalition Contract → coalition signature → edge product → archetype coalition → Guest Voice DNA Final Script → composition program → runtime embodiment → Primitive Evaluation Receipt and Activative evaluation → selective repair.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-169 — Query current Meaning and Experience Primitive Families

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_2`  
**Normative requirement:** Before script or composition strategy is selected, the Pipeline shall query eligible Meaning and Experience Primitive Families using source evidence, psychological role, tension, archetype, category, Brand Context Version, and execution stage.

**Trigger and preconditions:** An accepted Edge Product enters derivative planning.

**Required output or state transition:** A bounded primitive candidate field with activation, suppression, synergy, conflict, and misuse metadata.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Primitive retrieval precedes recipe selection.
- Meaning and Experience planes remain distinct.
- Primitive IDs are current and versioned.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a SuperVisual concept, when primitives are queried, then meaning-transform, delivery-shape, and format-material candidates are returned with reasons and conflicts.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a preferred layout template, when it attempts to backfill primitive labels after selection, then the route is rejected.
- **Evidence required:** Primitive registry queries, eligibility results, exclusions, and source-to-primitive rationale.

**Governing decisions:** D056, D058, D059  
**Exact source references:** SRC-DOCT-007, SRC-DOCT-008, SRC-DOCT-009

### FR-170 — Create explicit Primitive Bindings

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_2`  
**Normative requirement:** Every selected primitive shall be bound with plane, family, role, activation reason, source evidence, suppression conditions, misuse risks, and evaluation targets.

**Trigger and preconditions:** Primitive candidates survive selection for one derivative.

**Required output or state transition:** Versioned PrimitiveBinding records.

**Authority and invariants:**
- A primitive label without activation reason is invalid.
- Misuse and conflict metadata travel with the binding.
- Required bindings reference evidence.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given an Irony Inversion primitive, when bound, then its source contradiction, intended role, suppression conditions, and misuse evaluation are explicit.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a primitive chosen because it is fashionable or frequently used, when no source or coalition reason exists, then binding fails.
- **Evidence required:** Binding validation, source evidence, suppression tests, and primitive-role coverage.

**Governing decisions:** D058, D059  
**Exact source references:** SRC-DOCT-007, SRC-DOCT-008, SRC-DOCT-009

### FR-171 — Compile the Primitive Coalition Contract before recipe selection

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_2`  
**Normative requirement:** Primary, supporting, suppression, and conflict bindings shall compile into one PrimitiveCoalitionContract with coalition intent, signature, coverage threshold, misuse threshold, source context, and content hash before Steering Recipes or composition methods are selected.

**Trigger and preconditions:** Primitive Bindings are accepted for a derivative.

**Required output or state transition:** An immutable PrimitiveCoalitionContract.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Coalition precedes Steering Recipe.
- Coalition intent preserves psychological role and Edge Product.
- Conflicts have explicit resolution.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a Carousel route, when the coalition compiles, then the exact meaning transform, delivery force, progression function, format material, and suppression bindings are fixed before slide composition.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a Steering Recipe that has no compatible Primitive Coalition Contract, when retrieval returns it, then it is excluded.
- **Evidence required:** Coalition hash, coverage checks, conflict tests, recipe-compatibility tests, and operator inspection.

**Governing decisions:** D058, D059, D062  
**Exact source references:** SRC-DOCT-001, SRC-DOCT-009, SRC-CUR-020

### FR-172 — Emit Coalition Signature and Edge Product as measurable execution objects

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_2`  
**Normative requirement:** The coalition compiler shall emit the weighted family/candidate geometry, synergy, redundancy, routeability, and resulting Edge Product as separate measurable objects available to scripts, composition, evaluation, and learning.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A PrimitiveCoalitionContract is finalized.

**Required output or state transition:** CoalitionSignature and EdgeProduct records.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Edge Product is emergent, not a renamed primitive.
- Redundancy and fatality remain measurable.
- Routeability is category-specific.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given multiple surviving primitives, when the signature forms, then the system can explain which geometry produces recognition, humor exposure, mechanism reveal, or another Edge Product.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a coalition with high local charge but no routeable category expression, when evaluated, then coalition fatality is recorded rather than hidden.
- **Evidence required:** Signature vectors, routeability scores, fatality fixtures, and category crosswalks.

**Governing decisions:** D055, D058, D066  
**Exact source references:** SRC-DOCT-001, SRC-DOCT-005, SRC-DOCT-009

### FR-173 — Build Steering Recipes from primitive coalitions

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_2`  
**Normative requirement:** Steering Recipes shall be compiled or retrieved as execution strategies for a specific Primitive Coalition Contract, archetype coalition, composition state, embodiment, and known failure; they shall never act as the upstream source of the creative recipe.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A coalition and Final Script are approved and composition planning begins.

**Required output or state transition:** An eligible Steering Recipe set linked to coalition and embodiment.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Primitives build the recipe.
- Steering Recipes operationalize and repair it.
- Applicability and contradictory precedents are explicit.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a weak identity-anchor composition, when recipes are retrieved, then only strategies compatible with its primitive coalition, archetype, Visual DNA, and current geometry are considered.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a visually similar recipe that would suppress the coalition’s recognition edge, when ranking runs, then it is excluded or returned as a contradiction.
- **Evidence required:** Coalition-to-recipe crosswalk, hard negatives, retrieval receipt, and downstream decision lift.

**Governing decisions:** D058, D059  
**Exact source references:** SRC-CUR-020, SRC-DOCT-009, SRC-EXT-027

### FR-174 — Emit Primitive Evaluation Receipts and misuse/fatality diagnosis

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_2`  
**Normative requirement:** Each script, composition, provider plan, render, sequence, and repair shall receive a Primitive Evaluation Receipt measuring required primitive coverage, misuse risk, coalition integrity, Edge Product survival, and responsible repair layer.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A content-bearing candidate or final artifact is evaluated.

**Required output or state transition:** PrimitiveEvaluationReceipt plus pass, repair-required, or blocked decision.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Producer cannot approve itself.
- Coverage does not hide misuse.
- Repair preserves already-valid primitive relationships.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a polished SuperVisual with weak delivery-shape coverage, when evaluated, then the receipt identifies the missing role and a bounded repair target.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given high aesthetic scores but collapsed edge integrity or excess primitive misuse risk, when final evaluation runs, then the artifact cannot pass.
- **Evidence required:** Primitive coverage benchmark, misuse corpus, coalition fatality cases, independent evaluation, and repair replay.

**Governing decisions:** D059, D065, D066  
**Exact source references:** SRC-DOCT-009, SRC-DOCT-007, SRC-DOCT-008


## 7. Execution, model, tool, and human responsibilities

JIT Skill writers and Composers may draft and rewrite only inside the active Voice DNA, archetype, primitive, and source contracts. Programmed Models are bounded compilers or evaluators, not sources of doctrine. The operator approves the Final Script and any new creative boundary. Renderers execute composition programs and cannot invent the recipe.

## 8. Validation and quality gates

Validation must begin from primitive-specific activation, suppression, misuse, conflict, coverage, and coalition-fatality evidence. Primitive coverage, misuse, coalition fatality, source fidelity, psychological-role clarity, edge integrity, negative-space integrity, Voice DNA, Visual DNA, category grammar, and the active Activative Intelligence contracts are separate evaluation dimensions.

## 9. Risks, mitigations, and stop conditions

| Risk | Concrete consequence | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| Centroid flattening | The result is polished but carries no live tension or psychological role. | Enforce Matrix of Edging, coalition signature, Edge Product, CCV variation, and anti-centroid evaluation. |
| Primitive tokenism | Primitive IDs are attached after the creative decision rather than building it. | Require Primitive Bindings and Coalition Contract before Final Script and composition. |
| Archetype decoration | An archetype label is applied without its psychological geometry or sequence obligations. | Require an archetype coalition contract and approved Final Script. |
| Renderer-led meaning | The runtime chooses layout, motion, or imagery without the coalition recipe. | Renderer adapters consume only typed composition programs. |

**Stop conditions**

- No approved psychological role inside a named tension.
- No current Primitive Coalition Contract or archetype coalition.
- No approved Final Script before composition.
- Primitive misuse or coalition fatality exceeds the declared threshold.
- The output collapses source specificity, edge integrity, Voice DNA, Visual DNA, or category grammar.

This module becomes implementation-ready only after its FRs have primary vertical Story ownership, CBAR hardening has loaded the mapped Primitive Families and misuse modes, candidate Tech Specs identify exact brownfield contracts and tests, and a bounded Development Capsule is issued.

# F30 — Brand Genesis, Voice/Visual DNA, Distillation Layers, and Anti-Centroid Integrity

## 1. Product claim and user outcome

**User outcome:** Brand Context, Voice DNA, Visual DNA, RSCS, CCV, SDA, SFL, Source Fidelity, Negative Space, and Edge Integrity remain active through the entire source-to-artifact chain.

This feature prevents the source-first system from becoming a generic repurposing pipeline by preserving the guest’s linguistic and visual organism while expanding it through controlled variation.

The controlling Activative law is: **Content activates when it gives the viewer a psychological role inside a tension.** This feature must preserve that law from source interpretation through script, composition, render, evaluation, and repair.

## 2. Product boundary and ownership

The Atomic Harness Pipeline compiles and executes this behavior. Interview Expression supplies authenticated expression material. Builder supplies the category-native Harness. Studio supplies operator commands and approval. VAE supplies visual ingredients. None of these products may silently replace the approved archetype coalition, Primitive Coalition Contract, Final Script, or Activative Intelligence contracts.

## 3. Canonical objects and state

Core invariants:
- Brand Context Version is explicit and versioned.
- Voice DNA and Visual DNA are separate contracts.
- RSCS, CCV, and CBAR remain orthogonal engines.
- Source Fidelity, Negative Space, and Anti-Centroid integrity are measured at every handoff.

The feature emits immutable, versioned objects linked to source package, archetype route, Primitive Coalition Contract, Brand Context Version where applicable, Final Script, composition program, rendered result, and evaluation receipts.

## 4. Brownfield and doctrine-source treatment

| Source | Disposition | Exact path or reference | Role |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SRC-DOCT-001` | `ADAPT` | sources/MATRIX_OF_EDGING.md | Force selection, coalition signatures, edge products, and anti-centroid law. |
| `SRC-DOCT-002` | `ADAPT` | sources/CCP_ARCHETYPE_SYSTEM_MIGRATION_PROPOSITION.md | Archetype and derivative route system. |
| `SRC-DOCT-003` | `ADAPT` | sources/CCP_CMF_BRAND_GENESIS_AND_MICRO_SEMIOTIC_PIPELINE_V3.md | Brand Context Version, Voice DNA, Visual DNA, and Negative Space. |
| `SRC-DOCT-005` | `ADAPT` | sources/CCV_COMBINATORIAL_CONTROLLED_VARIATION.md | Controlled variation and coalition composition. |
| `SRC-DOCT-006` | `ADAPT` | sources/RSCS_RECURSIVE_SIGNAL_COMPRESSION_SYSTEMS.md | Signal saturation, collision, compression, evaluation, and recursion. |
| `SRC-DOCT-009` | `ADAPT` | sources/PRIMITIVE_COALITION_CONTRACT.py | Brownfield typed coalition and evaluation objects. |

These sources are migration and doctrine evidence. Their concepts must be reconciled into current contracts rather than copied as hidden runtime authority.

## 5. Workflow integration

Source expression → Matrix of Edging → primitive candidates → candidate survival → Primitive Coalition Contract → coalition signature → edge product → archetype coalition → Guest Voice DNA Final Script → composition program → runtime embodiment → Primitive Evaluation Receipt and Activative evaluation → selective repair.

## 6. Functional Requirements

### FR-175 — Load Brand Genesis Session and active Brand Context Version

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_2`  
**Normative requirement:** A brand-bound campaign shall resolve the accepted Brand Genesis Session outputs and one active Brand Context Version before script, visual research, primitive selection, or composition.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A campaign or derivative is associated with a brand workspace.

**Required output or state transition:** A pinned BrandContextBinding available to JIT Capsules.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Brand context is versioned.
- Historical versions remain replayable.
- Brand context cannot override source truth or Activative Intelligence.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a campaign for one guest brand, when composition begins, then the active Brand Context Version is loaded with its identity, visual, voice, micro-semiotic, and negative-space context.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given two active Brand Context Versions with unresolved precedence, when a job launches, then it is blocked pending operator selection.
- **Evidence required:** Brand version resolution, JIT inclusion receipt, replay, and supersession tests.

**Governing decisions:** D061  
**Exact source references:** SRC-DOCT-003, SRC-INT-001

### FR-176 — Apply Voice DNA and Visual DNA as separate composition contracts

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_2`  
**Normative requirement:** Voice DNA shall constrain linguistic cadence, syntax, pressure, intimacy, and anti-draft behavior; Visual DNA shall constrain identity geometry, visual constitution, material language, color, typography, texture, motion, and visual Negative Space.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A text-bearing or visual derivative is drafted.

**Required output or state transition:** VoiceDNAContract and VisualDNAContract bindings with evaluations.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Voice DNA is not a generic tone adjective.
- Visual DNA is not a moodboard label.
- Source fidelity remains upstream of both.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a guest with a reflective but confrontational voice pattern and tactile visual language, when content is composed, then text and visuals preserve those separate constraints.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a polished output using generic motivational copy or generic premium visual style, when DNA evaluation runs, then it is rejected or repaired.
- **Evidence required:** Contrastive Voice/Visual DNA fixtures, version pins, composition checks, and operator labels.

**Governing decisions:** D060, D061, D065  
**Exact source references:** SRC-DOCT-002, SRC-DOCT-003, SRC-DOCT-004

### FR-177 — Apply RSCS Distillation Layers before script approval

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_2`  
**Normative requirement:** The JIT script pipeline shall apply explicit Distillation Layers implementing RSCS saturation, collision detection, compression, evaluation, and recursion so that source density survives reduction into category-native copy and scene programs.

**Trigger and preconditions:** Source expression is condensed or rewritten into a derivative script.

**Required output or state transition:** A DistillationTrace linking source saturation, collisions, compressed claims, rejected generic drafts, and recursive revisions.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Saturation precedes compression.
- Meaning emerges through source-backed collision.
- Compression cannot invent missing signal.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a long interview answer, when distilled into six Carousel slides, then each compression step preserves irreducible signal and identifies the tension or recognition collision it carries.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a clean summary that removes all specificity and costly exposure, when RSCS evaluation runs, then it fails signal-density and reality-contact gates.
- **Evidence required:** Distillation traces, density benchmark, source-contact evaluation, and rejected centroid drafts.

**Governing decisions:** D056, D060, D066  
**Exact source references:** SRC-DOCT-006, SRC-DOCT-001, SRC-INT-001

### FR-178 — Use CCV for controlled archetype and composition variation

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_2`  
**Normative requirement:** Candidate generation shall vary explicit archetype, emotional register, Voice DNA register, intensity, audience maturity, representation geometry, and category-compatible composition axes while remaining anchored to RSCS-compressed truth and CBAR constraints.

**Trigger and preconditions:** The Harness requests multiple valid candidates or a novel category-native expression.

**Required output or state transition:** A CCVVariationPlan and diverse candidate portfolio.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Variation axes are explicit and separable.
- Novelty does not erase source truth.
- Candidates differ meaningfully, not only by seed.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given one Edge Product, when three SuperVisual candidates are requested, then they occupy distinct controlled coordinates while preserving the same source and coalition.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given three near-identical candidates that drift toward the same generic social aesthetic, when diversity evaluation runs, then the portfolio fails.
- **Evidence required:** Axis coordinates, diversity measures, source-fidelity checks, and comparative evaluation.

**Governing decisions:** D065, D066  
**Exact source references:** SRC-DOCT-005, SRC-DOCT-006, SRC-SPEC-001

### FR-179 — Apply SDA and SFL crosswalks to semantic geometry and delivery function

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_2`  
**Normative requirement:** The Pipeline shall resolve current SDA invariants, representation and archetypal geometries, plus SFL function, compression, surface, and failure-corpus crosswalks for the active archetype, primitive coalition, category, and output surface.

**Trigger and preconditions:** A Final Script or composition program is compiled.

**Required output or state transition:** An SDA/SFLContextPacket and evaluation obligations.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Semantic direction and delivery function are distinct.
- Surface adaptation cannot corrupt invariant geometry.
- Known SFL failure patterns become hard negatives.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a source-backed claim moving from video to Carousel, when crosswalks compile, then the invariant meaning remains stable while delivery function and compression adapt to the surface.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a surface adaptation that preserves words but reverses the archetypal geometry or overresolves meaning, when evaluated, then it fails.
- **Evidence required:** SDA ontology crosswalk, SFL profile, failure-corpus tests, and surface comparison receipts.

**Governing decisions:** D056, D059, D066  
**Exact source references:** SRC-DOCT-007, SRC-DOCT-008, SRC-DOCT-003

### FR-180 — Enforce Source Fidelity, Negative Space, and Edge Integrity across all handoffs

**Lifecycle:** `NEW_V1_2`  
**Normative requirement:** Every script, composition, edit, generation, render, and repair shall measure source fidelity, linguistic and visual Negative Space, focal and peripheral Edge Integrity, anti-centroid charge preservation, and the survival of the intended viewer role inside tension.

**Trigger and preconditions:** Any content-bearing state crosses a workflow handoff or is proposed for acceptance.

**Required output or state transition:** A DoctrineIntegrityReceipt with per-layer verdicts and repair ownership.

**Authority and invariants:**
- Centroid polish cannot compensate for lost force.
- Negative Space is active structure, not unused area.
- Edge Integrity survives source-to-script-to-composition-to-render.

**Acceptance scenarios**

- **Primary success:** Given a short-video edit, when evaluated, then the system proves that source specificity, reaction tension, visual asymmetry, peripheral cues, and the viewer’s role survived the final render.
- **Adversarial or denial case:** Given a technically correct and visually polished artifact that neutralizes the Edge Product, when doctrine evaluation runs, then acceptance is denied and the responsible handoff is identified.
- **Evidence required:** Cross-handoff doctrine receipts, anti-centroid benchmarks, negative-space metrics, Visual Syntax reparse, and operator calibration.

**Governing decisions:** D055, D056, D065, D066  
**Exact source references:** SRC-DOCT-001, SRC-DOCT-003, SRC-DOCT-004, SRC-DOCT-006


## 7. Execution, model, tool, and human responsibilities

JIT Skill writers and Composers may draft and rewrite only inside the active Voice DNA, archetype, primitive, and source contracts. Programmed Models are bounded compilers or evaluators, not sources of doctrine. The operator approves the Final Script and any new creative boundary. Renderers execute composition programs and cannot invent the recipe.

## 8. Validation and quality gates

Validation must compare source, script, composition, and render states rather than evaluating only the final surface. Primitive coverage, misuse, coalition fatality, source fidelity, psychological-role clarity, edge integrity, negative-space integrity, Voice DNA, Visual DNA, category grammar, and the active Activative Intelligence contracts are separate evaluation dimensions.

## 9. Risks, mitigations, and stop conditions

| Risk | Concrete consequence | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|
| Centroid flattening | The result is polished but carries no live tension or psychological role. | Enforce Matrix of Edging, coalition signature, Edge Product, CCV variation, and anti-centroid evaluation. |
| Primitive tokenism | Primitive IDs are attached after the creative decision rather than building it. | Require Primitive Bindings and Coalition Contract before Final Script and composition. |
| Archetype decoration | An archetype label is applied without its psychological geometry or sequence obligations. | Require an archetype coalition contract and approved Final Script. |
| Renderer-led meaning | The runtime chooses layout, motion, or imagery without the coalition recipe. | Renderer adapters consume only typed composition programs. |

**Stop conditions**

- No approved psychological role inside a named tension.
- No current Primitive Coalition Contract or archetype coalition.
- No approved Final Script before composition.
- Primitive misuse or coalition fatality exceeds the declared threshold.
- The output collapses source specificity, edge integrity, Voice DNA, Visual DNA, or category grammar.

## 10. Planning and implementation handoff

This module becomes implementation-ready only after its FRs have primary vertical Story ownership, CBAR hardening has loaded the mapped Primitive Families and misuse modes, candidate Tech Specs identify exact brownfield contracts and tests, and a bounded Development Capsule is issued.

*This feature module belongs to the Conscious Activations Atomic Harness Pipeline PRD V1.2 primitive- and archetype-centered reconciliation package.*
